< START > hypertrophy v strength training : what be the difference ?
there be some key difference between train for hypertrophy v strength .
hypertrophy refers to increase the size of the muscle , which be do by increase the overall volume of your workout ( set x rep ) .
strength train refers to increase the ability of a muscle to produce force , which be do through lift heavy weight ( above 85 percent of 1 rep max ) .
in short , hypertrophy be how big a muscle be , while strength be how strong a muscle be .
understand the difference between hypertrophy v strength training be important to understand since it be go to impact the type of workout and protocol you do in the gym .
in this article , i will explain : pro vs con of hypertrophy v strength train the difference between hypertrophy and strength training ?
who should do hypertrophy vs strength training ?
what be hypertrophy ?
hypertrophy be the physiological process of increase the size of muscle fiber through resistance training hypertrophy be the physiological process of increase the size of muscle fiber , typically in diameter , through resistance training .
there be two main type of muscle hypertrophy : sarcoplasmic hypertrophy and myofibril hypertrophy .
sarcoplasmic hypertrophy be what most people mean when they refer to hypertrophy training .
it be the physical increase of the muscle .
myofibril hypertrophy be when a muscle become more dense and compact .
these type of hypertrophy usually happen together , and so for practical purpose the distinction do not really matter .
but if you continue to read more about this topic , you will probably run into these term , which be why it be worth mention .
benefit of hypertrophy training below be four benefit of hypertrophy training .
note that many of these benefit can also be see with strength training as well , especially in beginner lifter .
build more muscle while both hypertrophy and strength training build muscle , the general consensus be that hypertrophy base training allows for great increase in muscle size and growth than heavy , strength base training .
hypertrophy training allow lifter to train in high volume , for long period of time , which have be show to be one of the most significant and effective variable for muscle growth less risk of injury weight training entail lift weight , and some injury risk be part of the process .
that say , hypertrophy training often have less risk of injury due to lighter load and less injury risk when training closure to failure .
increase energy expenditure energy expenditure can be increase by increase your output .
in other word , the more work you do ( training volume ) , the more calorie you burn .
hypertrophy training be know to have high level of set , rep , and overall volume , and therefore may be a great option for lifter who be look to increase muscle while also burn a ton of calorie .
this be not to say the heavy strength base program do not burn calorie , because they certainly do .
what it mean however be that lift with light to moderate load , with more rep , will equate to more work be do ( train volume ) , and that can increase calorie expenditure .
improves muscular symmetry hypertrophy training allow you to back off on focus on move a load from point a to point b , and really learn how to engage muscle , attack lag muscle group , and correct movement asymmetry .
when train with heavy load , it may be difficult to think about how the muscle feel or how to slow the moment down , as the load itself be one rep away from cruise you .
hypertrophy training give you the opportunity to build some more muscle awareness and improve muscle growth and symmetry , so that when it come time to lift heavy load you be in a more prepared and more injury - proofed state .
drawback of hypertrophy training below be two potential drawback of hypertrophy training .
note that these limitation be less significant with beginner , as they often can increase their strength at the same time they build muscle , and be often able to handle more volume simply because their absolute loading be often less than a more advanced lifter .
may not increase strength as effectively as strength specific training research show that the increase in muscle size ( often due to sarcoplasmic hypertrophy ) do not always lead to increase in functional strength of force output .
this be especially the case with more advanced lifter , and be why most lifter will train hypertrophy the farthest away from a strength competition to allow them to train hypertrophy properly , then shift back into a more strength focused program .
by do a program that progress from hypertrophy to strength , the lifter be able to reap the benefit of both training program .
could result in overuse injury without adequate recovery training hypertrophy mean you be often train in high volume , which may result in you train more than your recovery allow .
while this be often remedied by more sleep , more food , and a good training program that can track your progress and adjust as need base on your progress , it be still something to be aware of .
what be strength ?
strength can be define as the ability to generate maximal force through a muscle contraction .
strength be often demonstrate through heavy lifting and maxing out .
the ability to generate maximum level of force be dependent on a few key factor , such as : the central nervous system , rate of force production , and neural fatigue .
central nervous system the central nervous system be the control center for all movement and hard training .
it be make up of your brain and spinal cord .
when you train heavy , you train the nervous system to withstand heavy load without inhibit your ability to train hard .
the more your nervous system be prepare for heavy load , the less likely you be to pick something up and feel instantly tire or drain .
this be one of the main benefit of strength training and one of the more specific outcome of heavy training .
rate of force production faster rate of force production equate to more force be produce at once , which can help you move heavy load more efficiently , be more explosive , and break through stick point .
you can develop this by lift heavy load , as well as lift load with more velocity ( speed ) .
neural fatigue this occur when the central nervous system do not have enough recovery time due to lift too heavy , do too many set and rep , or train too much in general .
when neural fatigue occurs , you will often feel overly sluggish , have decrease performance and motivation , and will need to take often some time off , often week , from heavy training .
benefit of strength training below be two benefit of strength training .
while hypertrophy program can offer some beginner these benefit , more advanced lifter or lifter who have not do a proper strength train program will find that a more strength specific training program offer them these benefit .
increase neural drive and peak strength strength specific training increase the central nervous system be ability to send impulse to the muscle fiber to contract .
these impulse can improve the rate at which the muscle fiber contract ( rate of force production ) as well as how many of them contract at once ( fire synchronization ) .
both of these factor will allow you to move heavy load more efficiently .
can maintain or build strength while train less heavy strength training can help you maintain strength when cutting , mainly due to the central nervous system be stimulate under heavy load .
when people eat less , they often think they need to stop lift heavy , but rather , they should keep some heavy lifting in as they can not lose as much strength during a weight loss phase .
this be very important for strength base athlete who be lose weight for competition .
drawback of strength training below be two potential ( and likely ) drawback of strength training , especially when do in excessive volume , poor recovery , improper form , or lack of a deloading .
can lead to neural fatigue more easily than hypertrophy fatigue can happen during any period where you be train hard than you can recover from , however , neural fatigue often occur during high volume , high intensity ( load ) strength program .
while there be no clear guideline on what constitute something be too high in volume or intensity , as individual recovery rate can vary , it be often see when lifter train too heavy for too long or for too many reps. for example , do 6 - 8 set of 5 rep with 85 percent or more load on thing like back squat and deadlifts , and go to all out failure every set , multiple time a week , for week on end .
since the nervous system become much more involved when heavy load be lift , it can also be fatigue more easily at high intensity and high volume .
if you do overly tax your nervous system , the recovery process be much long than take a few day off of training , often several week until you feel fully recover .
neural fatigue be often a more serious issue with more advanced lifter or lifter who also have high stressor outside the gym .
may increase risk of injury and/or overuse injury lifting in high volume and train hard , no matter the training program ( hypertrophy v strength ) can result in some injury if proper form and recovery be not prioritize .
strength training , however , can increase injury risk and overuse injury , especially with poor recovery , high stress , and high volume strength program , as the loading be high than that use in hypertrophy program .
7 difference between hypertrophy & strength 7 difference between hypertrophy and strength the 7 difference between hypertrophy and strength be : training volume be high in hypertrophy than strength training total set perform be not significantly different in hypertrophy v strength program reps range be high in hypertrophy program than strength program load should be light when training for hypertrophy you can train close to fatigue more when training for hypertrophy compound exercise be best for strength development rest period can be as long as need for both hypertrophy and strength training volume be high in hypertrophy than strength train one of the main difference between hypertrophy training and strength training be the total amount of work volume accumulate within a session and program .
training volume can be calculate by multiply set x rep x load , and generally speak hypertrophy training be high in training volume due to the ability to perform more set and rep with less load than heavy , strength training .
this be not to say that you can not train in high frequency with heavy load , however , fatigue ( neural ) and overuse injury ( strain , tendinitis , connective tissue ) becomes much more of a factor when try to do heavy load in high volume .
total set perform be not significantly different in hypertrophy v strength program both hypertrophy and strength program will have a lifter perform 2 - 5 set of a give movement , however in some case 5 - 10 set may be program during strength training program because of the reduced number of reps. the total number of set perform can vary greatly base on the program , and be often not a key differentiator between hypertrophy v strength training , as rep and load be often manipulate to a great extent .
rep range be high in hypertrophy program than strength program hypertrophy rep range can vary greatly when compare to strength train rep range .
hypertrophy can occur in a wide variety of rep range , as the key driver for muscle growth be often train the muscle to fatigue and get the muscle burn , which can be do training in the 5 - 10 , 10 - 20 , and even 20 - 30 rep range ; as long as the muscle be take to failure .
if the muscle be not take to failure after 25 - 30 rep , the loading be too light to bring about significant improvement in muscle hypertrophy .
similarly , if the lifter fatigue prior to 5 rep , muscle damage be do , but not enough overall training volume can be accomplish often due to the lifter get generally tire before the muscle itself have be fatigue .
this be why most program recommend you to train in the 8 - 15 rep range to failure or very close to failure for best result if your goal be hypertrophy .
if you be look to increase strength , your rep range will often be between 1 - 5 rep per set , as the loading be above 80 percent of your maximum ( for example 5 x 5 workout at 80 percent load ) .
if you be train more rep than that , you be certainly increase muscle , however you may not actually be use heavy enough load to increase your strength maximally .
load should be light when training for hypertrophy training intensity refers to the load , more specialty how heavy it be relative to the lifter be maximum .
muscle hypertrophy occur use load between 30 - 80 percent of one be one - rep max , whereas strength training typically occur above the 80 percent of their one - rep max .
this be a key difference between the two , as you can have significant increase in muscle growth and size with light load ( 30 - 80 percent of max ) , however you need to lift above 80 percent to bring about the neural adaptation that take place to increase strength output .
you can train close to fatigue more when training for hypertrophy when hypertrophy be the goal , you can often train close to failure as the load be light and the failure be muscle failure rather than the body as a whole give out .
when look to increase muscle size and growth , local muscle failure ( such as what you feel in your quad when you do a ton of seat leg extension ) be the name of the game .
strength training be often more effective when you do not train to complete failure , as you run the risk of overtraining and injury as loading be much higher relative to your maximum .
compound exercise be best for strength development during hypertrophy training program , the goal be to train the muscle to fatigue , which can be do use a variety of load , rep range , and movement .
when train to failure it be often helpful to use machine and isolated movement as you can truly push the muscle to fatigue and not be limit by other muscle give out or form breakdown .
however , if you be look to increase max strength , you need to train movement that allow you to train with heavy load .
compound exercise be great for this , and the limiting factor for these will often be how heavy the load be rather than how much balance or coordination you need , or exercise that may not allow you to load up as much weight .
for example , do back squat with a barbell be much easy to load up 315lbs than it be to do kettlebell goblet squat with 315lbs .
research suggest that if you be train for maximal strength , you should prioritize movement that have you as stable as possible that be do with movement that allow you to load up with heavy load , whereas thing like bodyweight training , kettlebells , and isolation exercise may be best for hypertrophy or endurance program .
rest period can be as long as need for both hypertrophy and strength hypertrophy program may have short rest period than strength program because the loading be less .
however research suggest that long rest period for hypertrophy program may actually be more effective at allow individual to push to fatigue and increase muscle size , as short rest period may not allow them to push as hard .
they will feel tired , but the muscle may not be train as hard directly .
generally speak , rest period should take as long as it be need for the lifter to push as hard as they need to on the work set ( with the one exception list above ) .
if they can not perform as well as prior set , this be often due to not rest enough between set ( you will have some fatigue that set in , however this drop off should not be drastic ) .
who should do hypertrophy ?
strength athlete can benefit from perform a hypertrophy training program hypertrophy training go hand in hand with strength training , and be a necessary prerequisite for optimal strength development and injury prevention .
generally speak , lifter who be concern with gain size and muscle mass , and who be less concerned with maximal strength develop during their current training block can focus more on hypertrophy training .
they will still build foundational strength , and will be in a good position to transition to a more strength focused training program follow a few month of hypertrophy training .
strength athlete can benefit from perform a hypertrophy train program as a period where they can build more muscle , decrease stress and loading on the body , and help their body recover from prior high intensity training program .
this temporary shift in training focus could also lend itself to long term progress in strength development as well .
who should do strength ?
as state above , strength and hypertrophy go hand in hand and be critical phase of training for all lifter .
for lifter who be concern with peak strength , whether for athletic reason or competition , then they need to train with heavy load to have the nervous system adapt to heavy load .
strength - base lifter should however take a temporary break from lift heavy load every few month and enter a more hypertrophy focused training program to allow for more muscle tissue to be build and recovery of the nervous system and connective tissue to recover .
for lifter who generally do not lift heavy , enter a strength train program be a great way to add muscle and elevate your strength so that when you return to a more hypertrophy base training you will be able to continually progress , as at some point you will need to lift heavy to gain more muscle .
faq : hypertrophy v strength do hypertrophy also increase strength ?
for beginner and intermediate lifter , train hypertrophy will often increase strength , however in more advanced lifter a more strength focus training phase do after a hypertrophy phase be recommend if peak strength be the goal .
do hypertrophy make you big ?
generally speak , hypertrophy training increase muscle size .
while it can also increase strength , muscle hypertrophy increase the size of muscle fiber , as well as increase the amount of fluid push into the muscle to provide energy , refer to as sarcoplasmic hypertrophy ( generally do use high rep range and less load ) .
do you need to lift heavy for hypertrophy ?
no , you do not need to lift as heavy to gain muscle .
hypertrophy can be train with load between 5 - 30 rep , however muscle failure be a key factor .
for best result , experiment with the 5 - 10 rep range , 10 - 20 rep range , and 20 - 30 rep range to see which offer you the best stimulus to the muscle .
< END > < START > hypertrophy vs. strength training : a complete comparison weight training be one of the most important type of exercise you can do for your body .
whether you use free weight , band , medicine ball , or simply perform bodyweight exercise , train your muscle to become strong be beneficial for everyone – not just bodybuilder who be try to build a competition - ready physique .
research show that resistance training be associate with good cardiovascular fitness , resistance to injury and back pain , and reduce risk of diabetes and heart disease .
even a 20 minute session with dumbbell or circuit machine be enough to provide you with many of the health benefit of weight training .
when it come to train your muscle , there be two broad variety : strength training and hypertrophy training .
strength train refers to the type of lift focus on improve strength .
hypertrophy training refers to growth of muscle cell because of exercise .
it be important to note that these kind of workout be not mutually exclusive – many lifter will mix in hypertrophy workout along with their normal strength training routine , both as a new challenge and as a way to ensure their muscle do not get use to their normal routine .
however , at some point it be typically beneficial to decide if you want to focus on muscular strength or muscle size .
this article will go over these two idea , what they typically entail , and provide some recommendation on which type of weight training may be best for your personal goal .
what be strength training ?
as the name implies , a strength training program be one that be design to increase your strength , or the amount of force your muscle can exert .
unlike workout routine that be design primarily to add muscle mass , strength training focus on improve your ability to push , pull , squeeze , lift , squat and jump among other movement of the body .
some who participate in strength training focus on one or two specific type of lift , such as olympic powerlifters who compete in event to see how much they can deadlift or bench press .
to build muscle strength , you must perform exercise that break down your body temporarily so that more muscle fiber can be add in the `` damage `` area during rest period .
because they allow you to hit more muscle group at once , people focus on gain strength typically create a program of compound lift .
compound exercise often incorporate barbell or dumbbell and include exercise like : bench press deadlift squat military press besides the use of compound exercise , strength training be also distinct from hypertrophy training because of the way lift be program .
strength train usually involve heavy weight with a low training volume .
this typically mean you will perform a small number of set , but your lift will be high intensity since you will be use heavy weight .
also , as mention above , strength training focus more on compound lift that recruit big muscle as well as small tendon and ligament .
for example , bench press be a staple of many strength training program , since it utilize almost every upper body muscle include your chest , triceps , forearm , and others .
what be muscle hypertrophy training ?
while both hypertrophy and strength training will involve perform many of the same exercise with the same kind of equipment , the goal of hypertrophy training be a little different .
when your focus be on build the muscle tissue to be as large as possible , you will want to use a high rep range with light weight .
also , hypertrophy training emphasize isolation exercise that use only one or two muscle at a time .
some common exercise you would see on a plan focus on hypertrophy include : bicep curl quadriceps extension dumbbell fly hypertrophy - style training be popular in the bodybuilding community , where there be often a need to focus on muscle growth in very specific area to ensure the physique as a whole be ready for competition .
set perform in these kind of training session will also have high rep when compare to the kind of low rep , compound lift training that help cause strength gain .
because this type of training require light weight but more rep and set , it may take long than a traditional strength training workout .
you may also have to perform a variety of different type of move than you would on a plan focus on maximize strength gain .
a strength train workout with a barbell might call for only three or four different lift , while a hypertrophy plan may require six or more .
scientific research indicate that certain kind of exercise can induce hypertrophy in the muscle without a corresponding increase in strength .
which method be right for me ?
although these training method be different , neither be inherently good than the other .
many athlete incorporate both technique at different time , as their goal may change throughout the year .
here be a few tip for decide on whether your routine should be primarily base on gain strength or building muscle : if you be participate in athletic competition , you may want to focus on a specific type of strength training .
for example , soccer player might want to create a weightlifting program that help them get strong in their low body .
if you want to focus on get big in a specific area , such as your shoulder or chest , you might want to create a lifting plan that help you add skeletal muscle mass in these area through hypertrophy .
if you be new to lifting , you may want to start out with a focus on compound strength training exercise .
beginner have a tendency to add muscle quickly regardless of what kind of lift they do , and you may start out reap more benefit from compound exercise that use multiple muscle .
you can always switch to a training goal that be more focused on add mass once you gain more experience .
again , there be no reason you have to choose one or the other permanently .
many people mix it up .
on certain day they perform exercise with a limited range of motion that focus on activation of specific muscle group .
day , they will perform compound movement like lunge , deadlifts and pull - ups as a way to hit many different muscle group at the same time .
however you will still want to choose one main goal so that you know where to focus the majority of your effort .
final thought on choose between hypertrophy vs. strength training at the end of the day , both type of training be design to use the principle of progressive overload on the nervous system to break down muscle fiber so they can be rebuild strong , in a large quantity .
whether you want to focus on muscle building so that you can gain size , or you would rather improve functional , short - burst strength by focus on train fast - twitch muscle , perform some kind of resistance training be important for your health .
the cdc recommend perform muscle - strengthening activity that work all major muscle group at least two day per week .
whichever route you decide , by create a routine that work for your specific need , stay consistent over the long - term , and provide your body with adequate rest and nutrition , you can change your body and achieve your strength goal .
< END > < START > fast facts strength training and hypertrophy training be two different regimen that yield different physical result .
strength training increase muscle strength , while hypertrophy training increase muscle size .
the best choice between hypertrophy versus strength training come down to your personal goal and level of experience .
muscle strength and muscle size be definitely relate .
when you be new to lift weight , nearly any rep and set regimen will help you get strong and big .
but as you become a seasoned lifter , your result will begin to slow .
what once work ( everything ) be not help you pack on mass or strength like it be before .
what then ?
that be where tailor your training program specifically for strength or hypertrophy ( muscle growth ) can help .
what be the difference between strength versus hypertrophy training , which should you choose , and how to do it ?
if you want to build muscle mass , strength , or both , listen up .
hypertrophy versus strength training strength training and hypertrophy training be two distinct style of resistance training that each rely on different rep and set , weight , and exercise to achieve target result .
strength training make muscle strong , while hypertrophy training make muscle big .
here be how .
what be strength training ?
strength training be the best way to optimize functional muscle performance .
by train for strength , you will train your muscle be ability to produce maximal force .
to build strength , it be key to lift at heavy load .
to do it , drop your rep ( 2 - 6 ) , and lift heavy weight ( above 85 - percent of one rep max ) .
by cut the rep you will be able to focus on high - quality rep at more weight .
benefit of strength training strength - specific training will not just maximize your overall and peak strength .
here be a few of the other benefit you can expect : increase caloric expenditure and metabolism enhance athletic performance increase functional fitness increase bone density and muscle mass build or maintain strength while train less what be hypertrophy training ?
if you be look to visibly build muscle mass , hypertrophy training will yield the large size gain .
to enhance muscle size , it be vital to increase the overall volume ( reps and set ) during your session .
to do it , increase your rep ( 8 - 12 ) , and lift moderate to heavy load ( 65 to 85 - percent of one rep max ) .
by drop the weight , you will be able to squeeze in more rep per set in comparison to strength training .
benefit of hypertrophy training with hypertrophy , the aim be to achieve an aesthetic look by building big , bulky muscle .
however , that be not the only benefit .
a well - design hypertrophy program will also : increase caloric expenditure and metabolism increase muscular symmetry and reduce strength imbalance reduce risk of injury increase strength and power take note : strength training increase muscle mass , and hypertrophy training can also increase strength .
you ca not have one without the other .
but hypertrophy outperforms strength training for optimize muscle growth , and vice - versa .
which be well : strength versus hypertrophy training ?
there be no bad choice .
it come down to your goal .
if you want to increase the size of your muscle , hypertrophy training be for you if you want to increase the strength of your muscle , consider strength training should you try strength or hypertrophy training first ?
if you be a beginner , you should always do hypertrophy training first .
by start with hypertrophy early in your strength training career , you will be build both muscle and strength .
take your time to develop muscle mass , learn the proper technique , and gain some confidence .
when you do move on to strength training , you will have the muscle mass and technique to keep you safe when training at high load .
key difference between strength and hypertrophy training when it come to strength and hypertrophy training , each follow specific protocol for rep and set range , overall training volume , exercise selection , and nutrition .
here be the major difference .
exercise selection because the goal of strength training be max force production , your workout should center around multi - joint compound lift — like squat , deadlifts , bench press , and pull - ups .
but with hypertrophy training , you will want to use a combination of compound and isolation exercise to maximize muscle growth .
train specific muscle in isolation — like hammer curl , or leg extension — be not great for build functional strength , but it can be helpful in stimulate specific muscle group to grow .
your exercise progression during these phase of training should vary too .
since you work with light weight during hypertrophy training , increase set and rep , load , or add complexity to an exercise be all great way to continue build muscle .
because strength training relies on adequate overload , complexity be not your friend .
example of complexity include alternate arm and leg , or add a balance element to make an exercise more challenging .
often complexity take away from your ability to produce force .
instead , focus on increase your load or set to progress during strength training .
< END > < START > many , include bodybuilder , pursue muscular strength , endurance , and physique .
but achieve the desire outcome have become a challenge since countless training approach exist .
as a result , many fitness enthusiast have be leave ponder which path to pursue .
resistance training be one of the best way to train your muscle to become strong and big .
but as you begin resistance training , you realize there be two different approach to achieve these goal .
on the one hand , you have strength training focus on raw power and maximal force production .
on the other hand , you have hypertrophy training , which aim to stimulate muscle growth and sculpt a visually impressive physique .
the two popular workout be intertwine method but be different .
each approach bring its unique benefit and target different aspect of physical performance .
this article dive deep into strength versus hypertrophy to understand the fundamental difference between these train method .
what be hypertrophy ?
hypertrophy be increase or enlarge muscle fiber be size and volume result from target resistance training .
it be popular among bodybuilder who focus more on increase muscle size to achieve a visually impressive physique than strength and endurance .
like any other fitness goal , acute variable training , such as select exercise and technique , be crucial in achieve hypertrophy .
additionally , the number of repetition , intensity , set , and training frequency all create the ideal environment for hypertrophy .
they determine the stress level you must put on muscle to achieve your fitness goal .
hypertrophy training typically involve a high training volume of high repetition per set , range from 6 to 12 repetition at a low intensity of 75–85 percent of your 1rm , and multiple set , three to five .
this rep range be commonly associate with hypertrophy because it maximize time under tension , promote muscle damage and metabolic stress .
the training be perform use lighter weight with low intensity .
therefore , it may take long to see the result than a person do a strength training workout .
you may also need to do a wide range of movement that target specific muscle group from various angle than strength training .
the hypertrophy training routine should include compound exercise such as back squat , deadlifts , bench press , and t - bar row to recruit multiple muscle group simultaneously .
you may also need to incorporate isolation exercise , such as bicep curl or leg extension , to target individual muscle .
benefit of hypertrophy below be four pro of hypertrophy : increased muscle mass while hypertrophy and strength training increase muscle size , hypertrophy allow a tremendous increase in muscle size and growth .
this be because hypertrophy enables you to train in high volume ( do more rep and set ) for an extended period .
the high the training volume , the more mass increase .
enhance functional fitness and injury prevention although hypertrophy training be often associate with bodybuilding and aesthetic , it also have functional fitness and injury prevention benefit .
as the muscle increase , they provide good support and stability to the joint .
improved structural integrity help to prevent injury during physical activity and sport .
additionally , hypertrophy involve lift light weight which often have less risk of injury when training .
promotes muscular symmetry perform workout incorrectly can cause imbalance in muscle development .
by target specific muscle , you can address muscle imbalance use hypertrophy workout , which can help create a more proportionate and symmetrical physique , enhance aesthetic and functional ability .
increase energy expenditure one way to increase energy expenditure be by increase your training volume ( output ) .
and since hypertrophy involve perform more rep , set , and overall high training volume , it can be the best way to burn more calorie while increase muscle size .
hypertrophy con below be four drawback of hypertrophy : reduced strength and power while hypertrophy increase muscle size , it do not increase strength and power like strength training .
research show that muscle mass increase due to sarcoplasmic hypertrophy do not always increase strength or force .
overused injury hypertrophy training can place substantial stress on your muscle , tendon , and joint as it involve high volume , intense workout , and repetitive movement .
also , the training have short resting time .
without sufficient muscle recovery time between session , the body may be unable to repair and adapt , increase the risk of overuse injury .
focus on aesthetic over function compare to strength training , which emphasize strength and endurance , hypertrophy training often strongly emphasize aesthetic and muscle size , which may not align with everyone be fitness goal or functional need .
risk of overtraining due to high training volume and lack of adequate time to recover between workout , intense hypertrophy training can push the body to its limit , increase the risk of overtraining .
what be strength training ?
while hypertrophy be focus on increase muscle size , strength training be a type of resistance training exercise focus on increase the ability of your muscle to produce strength and endurance .
the workout mainly focus on improve muscle strength , power , and perseverance to enhance your ability to push , pull and lift weight , among other exercise .
to stimulate strength gain , the muscle must be subject to a level of resistance that exceed what they be accustom to .
the progressively heavy weight or increase resistance apply stress to your muscle , cause microscopic damage to the muscle fiber .
this damage stimulate physiological response that force the body to adapt to the increase demand , improve strength .
unlike hypertrophy , strength training usually involve lift heavy weight with low training volume .
this mean you perform few set of about 4 - 6 set per workout but with high intensity of 85–100 percent of your single - rep weight capacity .
the high intensity often improve with strength .
strength training workout usually target large and multiple muscle group and joint in one action to enhance overall strength .
these include muscle like the chest , back , shoulder , arm , and leg .
typical exercise include squat , deadlifts , bench press , shoulder press , row , lunge , and various upper - body and low - body exercise .
benefit of strength training while strength and hypertrophy training share common benefit , strength training have some distinct advantage compare to hypertrophy - focused training .
they include : increased strength strength training program often involve lift heavy weight at low repetition , aim to develop the neuromuscular system , improve the force production rate , and fire synchronization necessary for lift great load .
this focus on maximal strength can be particularly beneficial for you or athlete such as olympic power lifter involve in sport that require explosive power .
enhance neuromuscular coordination strength train improves neuromuscular coordination — efficient communication and synchronization between the nervous system and muscle .
by perform complex movement and progressively increase the load , strength training enhance the nervous system be ability to recruit and activate the appropriate muscle fiber , improve coordination and motor skill .
joint stability and injury prevention strength train target the muscle surround and support the joint .
this increase stability and reduce the risk of injury like sprain , strain , and instability .
con of strength training despite strength training have pro , it also have its con .
they include : increased risk of injury strength train involves lift heavy weight and perform complex movement under high intensity .
this can increase the risk of injury if proper form , technique , and safety precaution be not follow .
neural fatigue neural fatigue refers to a decrease in the ability of the nervous system to recruit and activate muscle fiber efficiently , result in a reduction in strength and performance .
lift heavy weight at high intensity , as in strength training , place significant stress on the nervous system , lead to neural fatigue , especially when training session be frequent without adequate recovery period .
hypertrophy vs. strength training which be the best ?
hypertrophy and strength training interconnect with each other .
when you perform hypertrophy , the increase muscle can result in an improvement in strength .
when you do strength training , the ability to perform workout for long period increase , possibly result in hypertrophy .
although these workout be interconnect , you can choose the one you want to focus on depend on your fitness goal .
focus on hypertrophy if your fitness goal be big muscle and a well - define muscular physique .
the training will help you add skeletal muscle mass in targeted area like your shoulder or chest .
if you be an athlete participating in athletic performance , strength training may suit you .
create a strength training program target the area you need to increase strength .
if you be new to lifting , the national academy of sport medicine recommend build a solid foundation through compound strength training before try hypertrophy .
besides , novice tend to develop muscle rapidly regardless of the type of lift they do .
thus , you may begin reap hypertrophy benefit from strength training compound exercise that use multiple muscle .
upon gain more experience and a strong foundation , you can switch to hypertrophy training if muscle gain be your goal .
also , you can mix hypertrophy and strength training exercise if you be advance in weightlift and want to improve strength and endurance alongside increase muscle mass .
for instance , you can perform hypertrophy workout with a constrained range of motion on certain day to activate and increase the size of specific muscle group .
on alternate day , you use strength training compound exercise like deadlifts , lunge , and press - ups to work for numerous muscle group simultaneously .
however , choose one main goal be still important to know where to focus most of your time and energy .
conclusion understand the difference between hypertrophy and strength training approach be essential to unlock your full potential and achieve your fitness goal .
strength training build a foundation of power , resilience , and functional prowess .
it empower you to conquer physical challenge , excel in athletic pursuit , and develop a body capable of efficiently perform everyday activity .
on the other hand , hypertrophy training delve into the art of muscle growth and aesthetic .
it sculpt and shape your physique , create visually impressive result that showcase your dedication and hard work .
embrace the difference in these training approach by dive into the world of strength and hypertrophy .
< END > < START > can you train to build strength and build muscle at the same time ?
that be a question you may have wonder .
if you look around , there seem to be a big gap between the physique of those who strive to only build strength , like powerlifters , and those who only strive to build muscle , like bodybuilder .
so , be it possible ?
the simple answer be a resounding yes .
strength & hypertrophy go hand - in - hand not only can you build muscle and strength at the same time , but those two thing go hand - in - hand .
in fact , these go hand - in - hand so much so that if you be to pick one as a goal , you would get some of the other as a byproduct .
what i mean by that be that if you choose strength as your main focus , you would still see muscle growth and if you choose muscle growth as your main goal , you would notice your strength increase .
there be no way to avoid this completely because the same principle use to build muscle be use to build strength and vice - versa .
with big muscle come the possibility of more strength and with more strength come the possibility of big muscle .
do not believe me ?
take a look at 8 time mr olympia winner .
obviously , his main goal be to build muscle and have the great physique on the planet , yet you can find video of him deadlifting over 800 lb and bench almost 500 lb .
the correlation between size & strength why be there such a correlation between size and strength ?
one reason be that because when you increase the size of the muscle fiber , there be more potential for them to handle the heavy weight , as there be simply more fiber to be recruit to handle the load .
this just make sense , as we typically associate big with strong .
in line with that , great strength mean a great ability to handle a heavy load , which should allow you to handle more volume than someone with less strength .
volume ( weight x set x rep ) have be show time and time again to be the driving force for size ( and strength ) .
so , if you can handle more weight , theoretically you have potential to build more muscle than someone weaker .
training for both here be an example : imagine someone with a one rep max ( 1rm ) of 225 lb ( 102 kg ) and another person with a 1rm of 315 lb ( 142.8 kg ) .
“ rm ” mean rep max .
theoretically , the person with the 225 lb max would be able to comfortably do set of 10 rep with around 150 lb ( 68 kg ) while the person with the 315 lb max would be able to comfortably do set of 10 with 205 lb ( 93 kg ) .
who do you think would build more muscle over time ?
obviously , the person lift the heavy load would be able to do more volume and would be more likely to experience great muscle growth as a result .
because of these thing , i would say that it be not only possible to train for hypertrophy and strength but that everyone look for either should train for both , at least to a degree .
since the two be not mutually exclusive , it be of great benefit to draw from muscle building and strength building practice .
so , if you be try to build pure strength , you should be look to learn some thing from bodybuilder .
if you be try to build massive muscle , you should be look to learn some thing from powerlifters .
a simple way to get the most out of your training for strength and hypertrophy be to vary the rep range you use in a week .
utilize low rep range with heavy weight as well as more moderate load with high reps. this will help you get the advantage of both .
of course , you can favor one or the other more depend on your goal , but the variation will definitely leave you good off than just do set of 10 - 12 for hypertrophy or set of 3 - 5 for strength every day , each week .
take - home message so , to recap , train for strength and hypertrophy be not only possible but unavoidable to a degree but definitely recommend .
by train for both in a week , you will allow yourself to get the benefit of both , which will help you whether you be look to primarily build muscle or gain strength .
< END > < START > hypertrophy training be when you train in a manner that promote muscle growth ( hypertrophy ) .
while there be various way to do this , the goal be the same : to increase muscle mass ( which may not be directly in line with increase strength ) .
hypertrophy training vs strength training for most individual ( beginner and intermediate lifter ) do a set of 10 back squat will both build muscle and general strength .
the key difference between the term come when you really define “ strength ” training .
for some , this mean just be able to lift relatively heavy weight .
for others , train strength mean train maximal strength , which be much more nervous system dependent than general hypertrophy training .
for this reason , most training that occur under the 5 rep threshold be often see as “ strength training ” due to the increase relative loading ( close to one be true maximum ) .
below , we will discuss various rep range for train hypertrophy , maximal strength , and general strength and muscle building : all of which be often accomplish in beginner training , but must be specifically attack at more advanced level .
rep range for hypertrophy when you be on a mission to develop big muscle and create more raw material to then transition into heavy strength training , it be important to understand the various repetition range that have be see to promote muscle growth ( which be not the same as maximal strength ) .
it be also important to understand that a lifter can get “ strong ” without actually increase muscle hypertrophy ( size and growth ) , which often occur early in a beginner be workout journey .
this be primarily due to increased muscle coordination and nervous system adaptation .
for this reason , many lifter will often train too heavy while attempt to maximize muscle growth .
for year , gym goer have be program to train 8 - 12 rep for muscle growth and strength .
while these be great recommendation for beginner ( and often where many people who be new to training should do ) , these be general guideline and do not apply as one begin to progress .
muscle hypertrophy when train muscle hypertrophy , various muscle group can respond to rep range differently base on generic , muscle fiber type , and the individual .
for example , individual with more slow twitch quad muscle may have good muscle growth training in the 12 - 20 rep range , whereas lifter who have more fast twitch muscle may just feel beat up training that high of rep ( and do not get delay onset muscle soreness ) .
in those individual , train a low rep range of 8 - 12 might suffice .
for most individual , it be key to experiment within the 8 - 15 rep range , and then work yourself either up to say 15 - 25 rep ( with hard exertion ) , and see what happen .
conversely , train with 5 - 10 rep can also be a good way for some individual to pack on serious muscle mass .
it be recommend however , that train less than 5 rep be reserve for more strength focus training .
hypertrophy this be a range that can be good for lifter who adapt good ( and get a good muscle pump and soreness ) use heavy load and 5 - 10 rep per set .
this be also a good in - between range for lifter who want to progress into a more strength - focused training phase , yet spend some time training in the 8 - 15 , or 15 - 25 rep range .
how to determine which rep range be best for you ?
this can be a challenging question for many lifter , especially when a friend have success do one thing , yet that same exercise and rep range just make your joint hurt .
below be three train outcome that you should look for when training for muscle growth .
if a movement , rep range , and workout provide all three of these , it be generally say that those movement and rep work well for your body and make - up .
1 – do your muscle feel pump up during the workout / set ?
this be instant feedback , and you need to focus on this during a set .
if you can not feel the muscle working , and feel the local muscle fatigue ( like a muscle burn or exhaustion ) , then you either need to lighten the load and focus on the movement , go slow and feel the muscle stretch , and use a fuller range of motion ( or good yet , do all three ) .
2 – do you have muscle soreness a day or two after the workout ?
delay onset muscle soreness be a key indicator of a good muscle hypertrophy session .
that say , muscle soreness be not always indicative of an effective training session , however some slight soreness can be a good sign of muscle stress that will then promote hypertrophy .
it be also important to note that soreness that impede your ability to train in follow workout , or one be that impair your day to day life ( like an overly aggressive workout that create severe leg soreness ) be a good indicator that you be on the right track , you just do too much volume ( too many set ) or train too hard for that session .
3 – be your joint pain free when do the movement ?
if at any point during or after a training session you have joint pain and/or discomfort , which be different from sore muscle , this be an indicator that you be cause too much stress and damage to bone , ligament , and tendon .
this can be cause by many thing , however the most common be ( 1 ) improper training technique , ( 2 ) too heavy of load , ( 3 ) lack of control in a movement .. slow down , and/or ( 4 ) injury .
if you be injure or feel injured , it be best to back off from the movement that cause pain , rest , and determine if you need to see a medical profession .
if pain go away , try perform other exercise for the same muscle group as sometimes a movement might not work well for you , despite it do well for someone else .
look for a workout program ?
the workout will adapt automatically to your level of recovery and rate of progress .
with over 600 movement and exercise videos , you can be sure to perform the movement correctly for optimal result .
take the guesswork out of your workout .
add hypertrophy train into a strength program < END > < START > below be four area where you can add hypertrophy train into a strength program .
it be recommend to train your strength lift first , when you be fresh , and then transition into hypertrophy training with emphasis on the key marker above rather than how heavy you be lift .
unilateral exercise unilateral exercise be a great way to increase muscle activation , hypertrophy , and address any muscle imbalance .
movement like lunge , split squat , single arm press , and single leg hip raise be all good option to choose from .
train these with emphasis on coordination , proper technique and joint mechanic , and feel the muscle should be of the high priority .
single joint movement movement like hamstring curl ( only joint moving be the knee ) , triceps extension ( only joint moving be the elbow ) , and chest fly ( only joint moving be the shoulder ) be all example of single joint exercise .
these be great to address specific weakness or highly area that you may want to grow more muscle mass .
it be not recommend to train these movement with low rep range , so aim to perform 8 - 15 rep on most of these movement , or more .
machine - base lift similar to single joint and unilateral movement , machine be a great way to increase muscle mass without have to place additional stress on supportive muscle group .
while that be generally a benefit for overall fitness , training in an isolated manner after compound strength lift can help target a muscle group without weak supportive muscle hold you back .
let be say for example , you want to grow your quadriceps more , so you attack 4 set of squat for strength .
afterwards , you could train high rep back squat , however you may find your low back fatigue out or you simply feel drain .
instead , perform machine hack squat may be a solid option as it can take pressure off your low back and allow you to isolate the quad more and provide more stimulus for growth .
light compound lifts you can train compound movement , often one you do for strength , for muscle hypertrophy as well .
just be aware that some movement , like high rep deadlifts , will create high amount of systemic ( and nervous system ) fatigue , and may not be the best option for muscle hypertrophy of the hamstring due to the overall stress it promote .
instead , you could train deadlifts for strength , and then move to a less stressful exercise like barbell good morning to specifically target the hamstring .
below be four tip to help you maximize muscle hypertrophy and aid in overall strength development .
1 – monitor training volume your accessory hypertrophy training should be do in a way that support your strength lift .
if you find you be beat yourself up from accessory exercise that cause more fatigue ( you be not recover from workout ) , and/or your strength be not go up , you may be perform too much training volume .
you can refer to this hypertrophy training guideline central hub for more specific recommendation of optimal training volume for muscle growth .
2 – understand your rep range be sure to refer to the rep range guideline from early in this article .
these guideline will help you navigate your accessory training program , and help you good individualize your own muscle growth goal base on how your body react to various rep range .
3 – understand positive marker for muscle growth when training for muscle hypertrophy , it be key to not focus on how much weight you be lift , but rather how your body respond to the stress of a training session .
use the 3 training outcome from above to help guide you along your muscle building journey .
if you find you be fail to accomplish all three objective , then you need to reevaluate your rep range , overall training load ( do too much or not enough ) , technique , range of motion ( fuller be well ) , tempo of movement ( slow and control on lower phase ) , and exercise selection .
4 – know when to back off your hypertrophy training should support your strength goal .
if you find that your hypertrophy training be ( 1 ) create excessive soreness that impede your strength training , ( 2 ) result in joint pain and/or connective tissue issue , or ( 3 ) general lack of recovery ; it be best to back off slightly and do one or two less set per movement and see if that help your body recover over a span of a couple week .
final note when training for muscle hypertrophy , be sure to always monitor overall training volume so that you can maximize muscle growth , allow for recovery , and still train strength .
add too much can certainly be counterproductive , but by follow the tip above you should be able to navigate those water .
lastly , it be also important to note that you can dedicate certain training phase ( 6 - 12 week in length ) to more hypertrophy - focused training , with the strength movement be there to maintain while you push hard on gain muscle mass .
this be often do , and then transition into a more strength - focused period .
< END > < START > maximize both can you get 100 percent of the maximum hypertrophy possible while also get 100 percent of the maximum strength possible , in short no .
there be a reason the top bodybuilder be more jacked than the top powerlifters .
it be not just body fat percentage difference .
there be a reason powerlifters be strong than bodybuilder ( when it come to 1rms ) .
maximize the amount of muscle on your frame be different to have a lot of muscle while try to be as strong as possible .
this be especially important the more advanced you become .
for a completely untrained person there be very little difference between train for maximal strength and maximal hypertrophy .
the more advanced you get the more this diverge .
there be always a trade off for be the best at something .
this do not just apply to lift .
decathletes be not world record holder in any individual event .
you only have limit resource , the specific training require to be the best at one thing take a massive amount of time , energy and recovery resource .
this mean that unless the other thing you be try to be the best at be very similar there will not be enough carryover to be near your potential at both .
100 m and 200 m sprint be a good example .
however this be also only possible due to how much of a genetic freak he be .
if he have only focus on one of them he would have still have be well at that one than when he be train both of them .
you can be world class at one thing and good at many others .
you will not be world class in several thing due to the nature of what it take to be world class .
diminish return it be well to think of strength and hypertrophy as a spectrum , if you maximize strength you ca not maximize hypertrophy and vice versa .
where in this spectrum your training put you will determine how strong you be relative to your size .
as state above you will not be able to get as strong and muscular as possible at the same time , but you can be pretty close to both .
this be a difference that will not matter much unless you be try to compete against others at an elite level .
this be due to diminish return .
you have probably hear of the pareto principle .
if not it mean that roughly 80 percent of the result come from put in 20 percent of the effort .
it do not necessarily apply in all case with those specific percentage but the principle stand well .
there be definitely diminish return .
when you get past a low baseline each unit of effort lead to small and small increase in result .
put number to this if 50 unit of effort get you 100 unit of result .
100 unit of effort may only get you 125 unit of result .
so a 100 percent increase in effort only lead to a 25 percent increase in result .
do not get attach to the specific number , the principle be what be worth note .
how do this apply to combine both ?
let say you have 100 unit of effort to give .
if you purely prioritize one this may give you 100 unit of result in that one and 60 in the other ( as there be carryover between both ) lead to 160 total unit .
if you give 50 unit of effort to both this may give you 90 unit of result in both ( carryover ) lead to 180 total unit of result .
try to balance both would give slightly bad result to either one individually , but good result overall .
this be what a lot of lifter who do not compete would like ( include me ) .
it do not even have to be 50 - 50. if you care about one more it be useful to know how to combine both .
this be all relative to your genetics .
you may try to get as jack as possible and put everything into it .
maximize the effectiveness of your training , diet , sleep , stress management etc over a ten year period .
genetic freak exist and can put in less effort for half the time and get good result .
this be an unfortunate reality but largely irrelevant unless you be compete in something .
all you can focus on be get the best out of yourself , if you have do that there be nothing more you could have do so why worry ?

i remember listen to this 2 - 3 month ago .

often “ new information ” be just old information put into someone else be word .
