< END > < START > benefit of barbell exercise 1. they be ideal for gain strength .
there be three main reason barbell exercise be ideal for build strength : 1. one of the best way to get strong be to train with heavy weight .
when you use dumbbell , you can only progress up to the heavy dumbbell available in your gym ( usually around 100 pound ) , but no far .
while this be plenty to progress on most exercise , it will not be enough to achieve progressive overload on exercise like the squat , deadlift , bench press , and dumbbell row after several year of proper training .
with a barbell , though , you can push , pull , and squat far more weight than you ever could with dumbbell .
not only be barbell physically strong than dumbbell ( some can hold over 3,000 pound ) , but they also allow you to put your body in a position where you can lift heavy weight more efficiently ( for instance , the barbell squat vs the goblet squat ) .
thus , you can get strong with barbell exercise far long than you can with dumbbell .
2. with most barbell exercise , you be able to use both hand to keep the bar stable and the weight evenly distribute over both the left and right side of your body , which make it easy to push and pull heavy load than with dumbbell .
for example , in the dumbbell bench press , you have to consciously fight to keep both of your hand about the same distance from your chest , whereas this mostly take care of itself when do the barbell bench press .
3. the exercise that allow you to handle the heavy weight , such as the squat , deadlift , and bench and overhead press , be easy to perform with a barbell .
you can perform these exercise with dumbbell , but once the dumbbell get heavy ( over 75 pound ) , they become unwieldy , awkward , and at time , unsafe .
2. they be adaptable .
barbell can be use for many different type of exercise , include ... bodybuilding powerlifting strongman crossfit olympic weightlifting ... which mean that no matter how you like to train , you can almost always use a barbell .
3. they allow you to perform exercise safely .
because your hand be “ locked ” in position during barbell exercise , you tend to have more control over a barbell than you do when you use dumbbell , which typically make exercise safer .
what be more , you often have to “ nudge , ” “ flick , ” or “ clean ” dumbbell to get them into the proper position to perform an exercise .
for example , in the dumbbell shoulder press , you have to lift the dumbbell onto your thigh then “ kick ” them up to shoulder height to get into the starting position .
set up like this be not so bad when the dumbbell be light , but it begin to feel unsteady and fatigue as the weight get heavy ( usually over 50 pound or so for men and 25 for woman ) .
get in position be not as precarious for most compound barbell exercise because they generally involve a power rack .
this allow you to quickly get into a safe and efficient position before bear any weight .
( use a squat rack also make it safe to drop the bar if you happen to hit failure on most barbell exercise . )
4. they allow you to increase weight in small increment .
increase the weight you lift over time — also know as progressive overload — be the most important driver of strength and muscle gain .
most dumbbell go up in 5 - pound increment , which mean when you increase the weight for a dumbbell exercise , you typically have to lift a minimum of 10 pound more than you previously do ( each dumbbell weigh 5 pound more than the previous one you use ) .
when you be new to weightlift , 10 - pound jump from week to week be easy .
as you nudge your genetic limit for muscle and strength gain , however , you will not be able to progress this quickly , and you will need to increase the weight more gradually .
most gym have barbell plate as small as 2.5 pound , which allow you to make small , more sustainable , 5 - pound increase that allow you to keep get strong without become plateaued or injure .
the 18 best barbell exercise for building muscle and strength this list of barbell exercise be far from exhaustive , but it include all of the best barbell exercise you can do for your entire body .
the best barbell chest exercise 1. barbell bench press barbell bench press the barbell bench press be one of the single best upper - body barbell exercise you can do because it train every major muscle group in above your waist , particularly your pecs , triceps , and deltoid .
how to : lie on a flat bench with your foot flat on the floor , directly under your knee .
pull your shoulder blades together and down , and without lift your butt or shoulder off the bench , slightly arch your back .
grab the bar with your hand slightly wide than shoulder width apart , take a deep breath , brace your core , and unrack the barbell .
bring the barbell to the middle of your chest , make sure to keep your elbow tuck at about a 45 - degree angle relative to your body .
when the bar touch your chest , explosively press the bar back to the start position .
2. incline barbell bench press incline barbell bench press the incline barbell bench press be one of the most effective barbell exercise for your chest because it emphasize the oft - neglect “ upper chest .
” include it in your chest workouts ensure you build proportionate chest mass— “ fill out ” your entire pecs .
how to : lie on a bench that be angle at 30 - to-45 degree and place your foot flat on the floor .
pull your shoulder blades together and down , and without lift your butt or shoulder off the bench , slightly arch your back .
grab the bar with your hand slightly wide than shoulder - width apart , take a deep breath , brace your core , and unrack the barbell .
bring the barbell to your upper chest , make sure to keep your elbow tuck at about a 45 - degree angle relative to your body .
when the bar touch your chest , explosively press the bar back to the start position .
3. decline barbell bench press decline barbell bench press research show that the decline barbell bench press train the low chest and triceps just as well as the flat barbell bench press ( though it do not train the shoulder quite so well ) .
this mean it be a good addition to your routine if you want a break from flat benching or if you want to use the decline bench press as an accessory exercise for your pecs .
how to : lie on a decline bench , secure your foot under the pad ( if available ) and adjust your body so your eye be under the bar .
pull your shoulder blades together and down , and without lift your butt or shoulder off the bench , slightly arch your back .
grab the bar with your hand slightly wide than shoulder - width apart , take a deep breath , brace your core , and unrack the barbell .
bring the barbell to your upper chest , make sure to keep your elbow tuck at about a 45 - degree angle relative to your body .
when the bar touch your chest , explosively press the bar back to the start position .
the best barbell back exercise 1. deadlift deadlift the deadlift train every muscle in your back , though it be a particularly good low back barbell exercise .
it also allow you to use some of the heavy weight in any of your workout , which mean it be ideal for gain strength and muscle .
how to : position your foot so they be a bit less than shoulder - width apart with your toe point slightly out .
move a loaded barbell over your midfoot so it be about an inch from your shin .
move down toward the bar by push your hip back and grip the bar just outside your shin .
take a deep breath of air into your belly , flatten your back by push your hip up slightly , and then drive your body upward and slightly back by push through your heel until you be stand up straight .
reverse the movement and return to the start position .
2. barbell row barbell row you can generally lift more weight with the barbell row than you can with other back exercise with a barbell , which mean it be a boon to any back workout for mass .
how to : position your foot under a load barbell about shoulder - width apart with your toe point slightly outward .
bend over and grab the bar with a slightly wide than shoulder - width grip and with your palm face toward you .
straighten your back and raise your hip until your back be roughly parallel to the floor .
initiate the movement by drive through your leg , then , use the momentum generate by your low body , pull the barbell to your upper body , touch it anywhere between your low chest and belly button .
once the bar touch your body , reverse the movement and return to the start position .
3. pendlay row pendlay row the pendlay row be a similar compound barbell back exercise to the barbell row , except you do not use your low body to help hoist the bar off the floor .
this mean you probably will not be able to lift as much weight as you do with other row variation , but it also mean your lat , trap , and rhomboid do more of the work and you be not limit by your low - body strength .
how to : position your foot under a load barbell about shoulder - width apart with your toe point slightly outward .
bend over and grab the bar with a slightly wide than shoulder - width grip with your palm face toward you .
straighten your back and raise your hip until your back be roughly parallel to the floor .
pull the barbell to your upper body , touch it anywhere between your low chest and belly button .
once the bar touch your body , reverse the movement and return it to the floor .
the best barbell shoulder exercise 1. standing barbell overhead press stand barbell overhead press the stand overhead press improve upper - body strength , chest , shoulder , and tricep size , and develop your whole - body balance and coordination .
how to : set a barbell in a rack at the same height as your upper chest .
grip the bar with a shoulder - width grip and your palm face away from you .
unrack the barbell and take a small step backwards with each foot , keep your wrist stack over your elbow , and your elbow tuck close to your side .
plant your foot just outside of shoulder - width , brace your core , squeeze your glute , and push the bar off your chest toward the ceiling .
once your arm be straight and your elbow be lock out , reverse the movement to return to the start position .
2. seat barbell overhead press seat barbell overhead press the seat barbell overhead press and the standing barbell overhead press be very similar shoulder barbell exercise .
however , because the seat barbell overhead press do not require as much full - body coordination , you can lift heavy weight and progress faster , which be generally good for muscle growth .
how to : set up an upright bench in a squat rack or power rack , or use a seated barbell press station .
sit in the seat and press your back against the bench , reach your arm overhead , and take a note of the height of your wrist in relation to the rack — this be the height you should set the barbell on the hook .
set the barbell on the hook , sit down , and grip the bar with a shoulder - width grip and your palm face away from you .
unrack the barbell and low it to your collarbone .
once the bar reach your collarbone , press the bar toward the ceiling and return to the start position .
3. barbell rear delt row barbell rear delt row the barbell rear delt row be a great exercise for train your rear delts , which be small , stubborn muscle that often need a bit of extra attention if you want them to grow as quickly as your other shoulder muscle .
how to : position your foot under a load barbell about shoulder - width apart with your toe point slightly outward .
bend over and grab the bar with a slightly wide than shoulder - width grip and with your palm face toward you .
flatten your back so that it be roughly parallel to the floor and let your arm hang straight down .
pull the barbell to your mid chest , make sure to flair your elbow at about a 60 - degree angle relative to your body .
once the bar touch your body , reverse the movement and return to the start position .
the best barbell leg exercise 1. barbell back squat barbell back squat the barbell back squat be hand down the most effective barbell quad exercise you can do for building size and strength .
it also allow you to use very heavy weight , which maximize tension in your muscle fiber and thus muscle growth over time .
how to : position a barbell in a squat rack at about the height of your nipple .
step under the bar , pinch your shoulder blades together , and rest the bar directly above the bony ridge on the bottom of your shoulder blade .
lift the bar out of the rack , take one or two step backward , and place your foot a little wide than shoulder - width apart with your toe point slightly outward .
sit down and remember to keep your back straight and push your knee out in the same direction as your toe throughout each rep. stand up and return to the start position .
2. barbell front squat barbell front squat most people think of the front squat as a quad exercise , but study show it be one of the best barbell glute exercise you can do , too .
what be more , research also show that the front squat place considerably less compressive force on your knee and low back , which make it a particularly good alternative to back squat for people who have knee or back issue .
how to : position a barbell in a squat rack at about the height of your breast bone ( usually an inch or two high than you would for the barbell squat ) .
grab the bar with a shoulder - width grip and your palm face away from you .
step closer to the bar so that it press against the top of your breast bone and push your elbow up and out in front of the bar .
with the bar resting on the front of your shoulder and hold in place by your hand , lift it out of the rack , take one or two step backward , and place your foot a little wide than shoulder - width apart with your toe point slightly outward .
sit down and remember to keep your back straight , elbow up , and push your knee out in the same direction as your toe throughout each rep. stand up and return to the start position .
3. romanian deadlift romanian deadlift the romanian deadlift ( rdl ) be a fantastic barbell hamstring exercise because it allow you to lift heavy weight , make it ideal for gain muscle and strength .
it be also less fatigue than other deadlift variation , so you can do it more often without wear yourself to a frazzle .
( fun fact : during a set of rdls , your upper back have to work hard to prevent your shoulder round .
this make the rdl one of the best barbell trap exercise you can do , too . )
how to : stand up straight hold a load barbell with a shoulder - width , overhand grip ( palm face toward your body ) .
flatten your back and low the weight toward the floor in a straight line while keep your leg mostly straight , allow your butt to move backward as you descend .
once you feel a stretch in your hamstring , bend your knee slightly more , and continue lower the weight until your low back begin to round — just below the knee for most people , and about mid - shin for those who be particularly flexible .
reverse the movement and return to the start position .
the best barbell arm exercise 1. barbell curl barbell curl the barbell curl be the most effective barbell bicep exercise because it allow you to use maximally heavy weight , which be beneficial for gain strength and muscle .
how to : while stand up straight , hold a barbell with your palm shoulder - width apart and face away from you .
your arm should be straight and the bar should be rest against your thigh .
bring the bar up to shoulder height by bend at the elbow , and then low it back to the start position .
( tip : to make this exercise more challenging and effective , raise the bar up to eye level , allow your upper arm to move forward , then low it to the start position ) .
2. close - grip barbell bench press close - grip barbell bench press the close - grip bench press be most people be go - to barbell tricep exercise because it allow you to safely and effectively train all three head of the triceps with heavy weight ( which can be difficult with other triceps exercise , like the skullcrusher ) .
how to : lie on a flat bench , pull your shoulder blades together and down , and without lift your butt or shoulder off the bench , slightly arch your back .
grab the bar with a shoulder - width grip or slightly narrow and unrack the barbell so it be directly above your chest .
bring the barbell to your low chest while keep your elbow tuck at about a 30 - degree angle relative to your torso .
when the bar touch your chest , explosively press the bar back to the start position .
3. lie barbell triceps extension ( “ skullcrusher ” ) skullcrusher the lie barbell triceps extension ( aka the “ skullcrusher ” ) be a great barbell exercise for arm because it train the slightly small medial and lateral head of the triceps , ensure you have define , proportional upper arm .
although you could say this exercise involve an e - z bar and not a regular barbell , an e - z bar be simply a slightly light barbell with a slanted grip .
how to : while lie on a flat bench , hold a barbell above your chest with a shoulder - width grip .
bend your elbow and low the bar until it be right above your forehead , and then reverse the movement to return to the start position .
( tip : if you want to increase the range of motion of this exercise , low the bar behind your head until it be almost touch the bench . )
the best barbell ab exercise 1. barbell landmine rainbow barbell landmine rainbow the barbell landmine rainbow be a great barbell core exercise because it force you to stabilize your core muscle under load , which build the type of core strength and stability you need if you play sport that require you to twist and turn at speed .
how to : place one end of an empty barbell in a landmine attachment or wedge it into the corner of the room and load the other end with weight plate .
while face the weighted end of the barbell , use both hand to hoist the barbell up to chest height .
press the bar overhead , then keep your arm straight , low the bar down toward your left hip , pivot your right foot inward as you lower the bar .
use your core , drive the bar in an arch until it be back overhead , then low it down toward your right hip , pivot your left foot inward as you lower the bar .
continue to alternate from side to side for the desired number of reps. 2. barbell rollout barbell rollout study show that the barbell rollout be an extremely effective exercise for train all part of the ab and core , especially the rectus abdominis and the oblique .
how to : kneel down on the floor with a load barbell in front of you .
with your arm fully extend , grab the barbell and slowly roll it away from you .
brace your core tightly so that your torso remain rigid and your low back flat .
roll the barbell until your body be as close to parallel with the floor as possible then roll yourself back to the start position by flex your ab .
tip : start with your knee and foot in contact with the floor , but as you get strong you can cross your foot and lift them off the floor a few inch to make the exercise more difficult .
3. barbell sit - up barbell sit - up the big benefit of the barbell sit - up be it be easy to add weight to .
be able to add weight to “ sit - up ” exercise increase their effectiveness and allow you to take advantage of progressive overload ( which be the most important driver of muscle growth ) .
how to : lie on a sit - up bench with your foot wedge under the foot pad .
use both hand , hold a barbell directly above your chest with your arm straight .
keep your arm perpendicular to the floor and your back flat , use your ab muscle to lift your chest toward the ceiling until your low back come completely off the bench .
reverse the movement and return to the start position .

the best barbell movement when we look at the human body , there be several primary movement that we want to try to replicate , make pull exercise , push workout , squat , lunging , and hinge crucial for any routine .
vertical pulling : we be start with the only movement impossible to replicate with a barbell , and that be vertical pulling .
vertical pull refers to exercise in which the arm grab an object from overhead and pull it toward the body .
horizontal pulling : horizontal pulling be when you pull an object toward your body .
all of the back muscle and biceps be involve in horizontal pulling .
vertical push : vertical push occurs when you have an object overhead such as in the overhead press when you press the barbell overhead .
the muscle train be the shoulder , chest , and triceps .
horizontal push : horizontal push occurs when you push an object away from the body , such as in the bench press .
the muscle train be the chest , shoulder , and triceps .
squat : many people confuse squat and hip - hinge .
the main distinguishing factor be movement and flexion of the knee .
when the knee come forward and involve more knee extension ( quadriceps activation ) , it be a squat .
hip - hinge : compare to the squat , in a true hip - hinge , the knee stay stationary and the shin vertical .
the primary joint be the hip , with the posterior muscle be the primary mover .
the main muscle work be the glute and hamstring .
however , the erector spinae often play a role in many hip - hinge movement .
lunge : a lunge be a movement in which a person take a step forward with one foot and then lower the body .
lunge exercise train every muscle in the low body as well as improve balance .
there be also several type of lunge , such as the reverse lunge , which will hit the muscle differently .
the best barbell exercise for upper and low body training we will break down the best barbell exercise into the upper and low body to keep thing organize .
top upper body barbell exercise first on the list be the best barbell exercise for the upper body .
these barbell exercise will train the muscle that make up the chest , shoulder , back , and arm .
1. overhead press : straight bar workouts the stand barbell overhead press be probably the most underused barbell movement on this list , likely due to its difficulty .
it involve press a load barbell straight overhead from the chest , and lock out the arm .
a cool fact about the overhead press be that it be actually an original movement in olympic weightlifting .
it be eventually take out due to difficulty keep standard for correct form ( athlete begin bend the back to extreme ) , but its legacy remain .
the overhead press might be the most challenging barbell exercise there be , but it will cause your upper body strength to blow up .
worth it !
how to do the overhead press : set up an empty barbell on a rack .
the bar should be place low than shoulder height around the middle pecs .
you do not want to get on your tippy toe , so if you have to choose , set the bar so it be near your low pec muscle rather than your upper chest .
place your hand shoulder - width apart use an overhand grip .
get under the barbell with your elbow push in front of the barbell .
your thumb should be touch the outside of the shoulder with the barbell rest on the clavicle and deltoid .
extend your leg , unrack the barbell , and take 2 step back .
at this point , be sure the barbell be rest on your body .
many new lifter will hold the barbell off the chest , which eat up energy .
tighten the core muscle and glute to create a firm base .
when ready , drive the straight barbell overhead .
as the bar reach the head , tuck it back until the bar pass and then pop it back in place .
this allow the barbell to travel in a straight line .
finish drive the bar straight above the head until your elbow be extend with the weight overhead .
2. barbell bench press : barbell bench exercise let be get into the horizontal press now .
perhaps the most popular barbell exercise , the barbell bench press be also one of the most misunderstood .
it be an amazing movement to improve the push strength and the upper body be overall musculature .
however , it be not necessarily the great chest movement as many make it out to be .
the flat barbell bench press do train the chest , but it be actually more effective in increase the size and strength of the triceps .
still , it remain one of the best barbell exercise because it be fundamental in provide a solid base to work from .
you can also adjust your hand position , change your barbell bench press grip to target different upper body muscle during the exercise .
we will also include several variation after our how - to , along with any modification you need to make .
how to do the barbell bench press : set up a bench and load the barbell .
lay down on the bench with your eye directly beneath the barbell .
grab the barbell wider slightly than shoulder - width apart .
the barbell should sit in the crease of the thumb .
to do this , reach your hand around the barbell .
this will help keep your wrist straight during the movement .
before unracking the barbell , dig your shoulder blade into the mat .
next , tuck your foot back .
this do not need to be extreme , but you should have minimal tuck .
this position cause your body to become much more stable and solid .
unrack the barbell and bring it forward , so your arm be straight .
this place it above your upper chest .
slowly low the barbell down toward your low chest .
this mean the barbell bench press be one of the few exercise in which the barbell do not travel straight .
as the barbell lower , keep your elbow tuck at a 45 - degree angle .
let the barbell touch your chest and then drive it back up .
as you drive the barbell up , it make a `` j `` as it travel up and back .
incline barbell bench press variation : most will put the bench at 45 - degree angle .
however , play around with small angle as well .
the only difference be the barbell will come down high on your chest , and the incline will hit the upper chest more .
decline bench press variation : again , experiment with various angle but the max should be 45 - degree .
the barbell will come down on your low chest , and the decline will target the low chest to a high degree .
close grip bench press variation : for the close grip bench press , grab the barbell slightly narrow than shoulder width apart .
as the barbell come down , be sure to tuck your elbow .
this create great flexion of the elbow while lessen the activity of the chest .
wide grip bench press variation : place your hand wider than a traditional grip .
this will cause less flexion in the elbow and great activation in the chest .
3. barbell bent over row : exercise with barbell weight let be hit those back muscle now , shall we ?
the barbell bent over row should be your primary exercise for build your back muscle .
it be really that simple .
this single movement be go to hit every single muscle in your entire back .
if that be not enough , the bent - over row do a lot more , include train your biceps , particularly with an underhand grip , require an intense isometric contraction in your posterior chain ( erector spinae , glute , hamstring ) , and need total core activation to support be bent over .
there be several barbell bent over row grip , and utilize all of them will help you target each of the major back muscle differently .
pay attention to the start position for the bent - over row .
it tend to be very difficult for some people , so take your time when first training .
how to do the barbell bent over row : load a barbell on the ground and stand in the middle with a comfortable stance .
your foot should be somewhere between shoulder width apart and hip width stance .
bend down and use and grab the barbell with hand slightly wide than shoulder - width apart and an overhand grip .
this prep portion should look similar to a deadlift .
stand up erect .
now time for the starting position .
push the hip back slightly and lean your torso forward while bend your knee slightly .
pull your shoulder blade back to maintain a straight , ridge back .
keep come down while keep a slight bend in your knee .
you must drop the torso forward enough that the arm hang freely in front of your knee .
try to get your torso as parallel to the ground as possible .
the more parallel you get , the more emphasis you place on the back .
when ready , brace and pull the barbell up to the belly .
as you pull , have your elbow bent at a 45 - degree angle .
think about pull your elbow to the ceiling rather than pull the barbell up .
this will encourage proper form and maximal use of the back muscle .
pull all the way up and then slowly low the barbell .
variation : use an underhand grip shoulder width apart , which be more narrow than the traditional grip .
your arm should slide against your body straight back , create great flexion in the elbow ( great bicep activation ) and increase your range of motion .
top low body barbell exercise now , it be time for the low half .
when use a barbell to train the low body , you will hit every muscle in every movement .
however , we still have more than one exercise due to how different movement activate the muscle differently .
1. barbell back squat : type of barbell lift the barbell back squat be the king of low body exercise .
it train the entire low body while place huge stress on the core ( in a good way ) .
the barbell back squat be the best exercise to create strength in the low body .
often see as a competition with the deadlift , these two be separate , but equally awesome , exercise .
that say , we rank it as the no .
1 low body exercise simply because of the much large range of motion see in the knee and hip .
far , the back squat also require significantly more mobility in your low body joint .
how to do the barbell back squat : set up a barbell on either a squat rack or power rack slightly low than shoulder height .
again , you do not want to have to get on your tippy toe to unrack the barbell .
place hand wide than shoulder - width apart with an overhand grip .
get under the barbell and place it on the upper portion of your back at shoulder level .
it should lay across your trap .
unrack the barbell and take two step back .
brace your core and push your hip back to begin the movement .
as you low , aim to have the bar drop straight down .
maintain a tight core and straight back the whole time .
continue drop your hip back but allow your knee to travel forward , ensure they always track over your toe .
continue until the top of your thigh break parallel , and drive back up by push your foot down .
2. barbell deadlift : bar bench workout if the barbell back squat be the king of low body exercise , that would mean the deadlift be the king of all exercise .
while there be definitely room for debate on this , the deadlift be arguably the best of the best barbell exercise .
implement the deadlift into your regular program will greatly strengthen and develop a ton of your major muscle group .
generally list as a low body exercise , the deadlift really stress the entire body , primarily the low body and back .
how to do the barbell deadlift : load a barbell on the ground .
stand next to the barbell with your foot shoulder - width apart .
most people stand too wide so pay attention to this .
the barbell should be over your midfoot and an inch or so away from your shin .
push your hip back to lower your body .
as you low , your shin will come forward slightly and make contact with the barbell .
however , they should be relatively vertical .
continue drop your body so your shoulder drop straight down until you can grab the barbell .
grab the barbell , so your hand be just outside your leg .
pull your shoulder blade back and push your chest forward .
your back should be tight and straight .
be sure to have your foot flat on the ground with your weight spread evenly across your foot .
your arm should parallel your shin and all your joint `` tight .
`` this be the starting position .
when ready , brace your core and drive your foot down to the ground to pull the bar straight up your leg to the knee .
at this point , your back should be at the same angle .
once the barbell pass your knee , you begin to drive your hip forward until your body be erect .
slowly low the weight go down .
use a big weight , you can do a control drop .
you let the bar drop but give some guidance and resistance .
this be to minimize bounce or the bar get away .
there be very few situation in which drop the bar be acceptable .
snatch grip deadlift variation : an effective and easy variation be widen your bar grip and use a snatch grip .
this be roughly 1.5 time your normal grip .
it do not need to be exact , so an easy method be to place your index or middle finger on the outermost ring .
from here , everything else remain the same .
3. barbell hip thrust : barbell rod exercise interestingly , the barbell hip thrust be the only single joint exercise on this list .
however , that joint be the hip and utilize the strong muscle in the human body , the glute .
this mean the load can be place directly on the joint in the hip crease provide a direct force .
in fact , this be the only exercise that do this .
that say , it be basically universally agree that it be the best glute exercise .
how to do the barbell hip thrust : set up a steady bench .
sit in front with your knee bent and upper back dig in the bench .
place a barbell in your hip crease and place your hand on the barbell for balance .
when ready , drive your heel into the ground and drive your hip up .
continue until your torso be 100 percent extend .
slowly low and repeat .
4. barbell forward lunge : full body barbell workout the barbell lunge will switch thing up a bit as it be the only unilateral exercise on this list .
while both leg be involve , the primary muscle activate only occur in one leg .
than give you the ability to identify muscular imbalance , the lunge be perfect for improve balance and move a weight under motion .
how to do the barbell forward lunge : place a barbell on your back or front , similarly to either the front squat or back squat , depend on your preference .
hold the barbell at least wide than shoulder - width apart to help balance .
stand with a neutral stance .
take one big step forward .
you may need to play around to get the right distance .
keep your toe straight , low your body straight down .
as you low to the ground , your knee should begin to form a 90 - degree angle , and the front shin and rear thigh should be vertical as the rear knee hit the floor .
push off the forward leg , return it back to standing .
repeat on the opposite side .
5. barbell front squat : long bar exercise do not be confuse .
when it come to front squat vs. back squat , both may be barbell squat but be rather different in biomechanics and muscle activation .
the front squat get its name as the barbell be place on the front of the body rather than on the back ( which make sense ) .
even though this may only mean the bar placement differs by a few inch , those inch cross the body be center of gravity .
as a result , the body be biomechanics be drastically alter as the body lower to keep the bar over the ankle straight .
for this to occur , the torso remain much more vertical with less hip flexion .
this should create high activation in the quadriceps but the data actually be not that clear .
however , one major benefit be there be less force on the spine² .
plus , there be also serious activation of the core muscle and upper back to prevent it from flop over .
in fact , study even show it generate more muscle activity in the shoulder muscle compare to an overhead squat³ !
how to do the barbell front squat : rack a barbell so that it sit at about mid - chest level .
walk up to the barbell and bend down to get under it .
lift your arm out straight in front of you .
this will cause your anterior deltoid to cause a lump .
the barbell will sit behind this lump .
flex your elbow and reach back to balance the barbell with your hand .
stand up , keep your elbow point out straight .
this be call the front rack position .
step back with foot flat and hip - width apart .
push your hip back to squat .
your torso will remain upright during the front squat to keep the barbell over your foot .
continue drop until the top of your thigh hit parallel .
power back up .
as you rise , focus on drive your elbow up .
this will help maintain an erect torso .
6. barbell romanian deadlift : barbell use the last low body exercise be the romanian deadlift .
this hip hinge movement have a similar movement pattern as the deadlift and use the same muscle .
there be a few major difference , however , include that the start position begin with standing , the hip have great flexion , and the knee be slightly bent .
and finally , the load barbell never touch the ground .
as a result , the romanian deadlift be a much more effective exercise to hit the posterior chain .
how to do the barbell romanian deadlift : load a barbell and stand with foot shoulder - width apart .
low down and grab the bar with an overhand shoulder - width grip or slightly wide .
stand up with a form similar to a deadlift .
this be the starting position .
take a deep breath , and push your hip back , keep a minimal bend in the knee .
pull your shoulder blade back to maintain an erect and ridge back .
start to slowly low the barbell in a straight line down your body .
it do not need to touch your body but should remain close .
as you low , think about build tension in the glute and hamstring .
continue lower but keep the knee slightly bend .
the goal be not to reach the ground but to build tension in the posterior chain .
low until you at least pass the knee slightly .
from here , continue but once your form begin to break , stop .
the easy sign be your back will begin to round , and your shoulder blade will come forward .
once this start to happen , stop .
begin come back up but concentrate on drive your hip forward .
we like to do the concentric portion explosively .
push your hip forward until you be erect back in the starting position .
variation : you can also use the snatch grip with the romanian deadlift .
power barbell exercise every athlete need some power in their training .
here be two of our favorite .
1. power clean and jerk : barbell bench press lie the clean and jerk be an amazing power exercise , combine two movement into one of the most challenging barbell exercise .
while it can take some time to learn , it would benefit any athlete who put in the time and want to improve their strength and lean body mass .
the power clean be easy to perform compare to a full clean as you do not need to drop into a squat .
how to do the power clean and jerk : set up similar to a deadlift but use a grip slightly wide than shoulder width .
push your chest up far so it be more vertical .
you may need to sink your hip more .
begin the movement by drive your foot into the ground and drive up .
your back will remain at the same angle until the barbell pass the knee .
at this point , perform triple extension and forcefully push your hip forward to extend your joint .
immediately perform a power shrug by shrug and allow the barbell to travel up your body .
be sure to bring your elbow up high .
as the bar travel up , drop into a 1/4 squat and pull your body under the bar .
flip your elbow up and catch the barbell in the front rack position .
fully extend your knee .
now , drop slightly ( no more than 1/4 squat ) and then forcefully extend your hip to drive the barbell up .
use your arm to help drive the bar completely overhead as you split your leg so one be in front of the other .
make sure the front leg be fully extend , while the back leg be flex slightly .
fully straighten your arm , fully lock the bar overhead .
2. snatch grip high pull : power barbell exercise the snatch grip high pull a highly effective power movement .
also , it will build a crazy strong upper back .
we like it because it be much simpler to perform than other olympic movement .
at the end of the day , it be a clean without actually catch the bar .
how to do the snatch grip high pull : grab the barbell in a similar manner to the snatch grip deadlift .
you can move the grip slightly narrow if need .
one difference be you want to try to get your chest up high , so you may need to sink your hip low .
begin drive up by drive your foot into the ground .
your upper body will remain the same until the barbell hit your knee .
at this point , you will forcefully implement triple extension drive your hip forward .
as soon as you hit extension , you be perform a power shrug and pull the barbell high .
be sure to keep your elbow elevate high .
instead of catch the barbell , you will simply let it fall to the ground use a control drop .
the best barbell core exercise you probably be not expect to see a core exercise on here , but - surprise !
most barbell exercise people speak about be those perform for the upper and low body .
however , this single barbell exercise be likely the only core exercise you will need to do .
that be why there be only one .
1. the barbell rollout : power barbell workout who need dumbbell ab exercise when you have the barbell rollout ?
the barbell rollout be a rollout do on a barbell rather than one of those little plastic toy .
while those would work , use the barbell have two unique advantage : 1 ) you can add weight plate to load the barbell and increase the intensity , and 2 ) the barbell allow wide hand placement for those who lack shoulder mobility .
how to do the barbell rollout : load a barbell and place it on the ground .
kneel behind it and place your hand wider than shoulder - width apart use an overhand grip .
if your shoulder joint have poor mobility , use a wider grip .
get your entire body over the barbell with your arm straight .
keep your core tight and begin to let the barbell roll out in front of you .
as you low , begin to push the barbell out in front of the body .
continue move down until your body be erect .
you should be very close to the ground .
use your core , pull yourself back up .
barbell rollout tip : a few thing to keep in mind : you can not perform this with an empty barbell .
you can only use full - size plate with a metal ring .
and , eventually , you want to progress to do them stand .
barbell train tip the above barbell exercise be all you need to get an awesome workout in , especially when you manipulate your training variable , switch up thing like hand grip .
below be some workout tip to help you make the most of your barbell training , whether you be focus on barbell leg exercise or barbell back exercise .
1. include both strength and hypertrophy : the general public often try to combine strength and hypertrophy , but they be two different physiological adaptation .
when discuss strength training vs. hypertrophy , strength training refers to improve the intramuscular system and make the exist muscle function good together .
as a result , you become strong .
this be best do with load of 85 - 95 percent 1rm and rep of 5 - 1. for average lifter , 85 percent be generally heavy enough .
hypertrophy training refers to the actual muscle get large .
this may or may not include strength gain .
the primary driver for muscle hypertrophy be volume and be best do with load of 70 - 80 percent 1rm ( or less ) with load of 8 - 12 , or more .

below , we will explore the best exercise for your health and how you can start work out .
first of all , how much exercise do you need ?
accord to the center for disease control and prevention ( cdc ) , adult should aim for 150 minute of moderate - intensity aerobic physical activity or 75 minute of vigorous - intensity every week .
during moderate - intensity aerobic activity , you should feel out of breath , but still be able to hold a conversation .
dancing , tread water , canoe and yoga be great example of moderate - intensity aerobic activity .
in vigorous - intensity aerobic activity , you will be too wind to speak more than a few word at a time .
jogging at a fast pace , bike uphill , jump rope and cross - country skiing be great example of vigorous - intensity aerobic activity .
the cdc also recommend that adult include activity that strengthen muscle , like weightlift , on two or more day of the week .
while all this may seem like a lot , how you spread your exercise time throughout the week be up to you .
you could work out for 30 minute five time a week , fit in hour - long workouts three time a week , or do fast - pace hiit ( high - intensity interval training ) workouts for 15 minute five time a week .
you can decide what work best for you .
what be the type of exercise ?
if you be new to exercise , you may want to try several different kind of physical activity to discover what you like .
remember , do not only focus on what kind of movement you can do , but also ask yourself what kind of movement you enjoy do .

man and woman laughing and chat while rid exercise bike in a gym .
cardio cardio , also call aerobic exercise , be any form of movement that get your heart rate up , your blood pumping and your lung work .
it activate and strengthen your cardiovascular system , but also improve the health of your whole body and mind .
cardio can lower stress , improve sleep and flood your brain with those feel - good endorphin .
it be also an excellent tool when it come to weight loss .
cardio can be the most easily accessible form of exercise – and the simplest .
a brisk walk or yard work can count as cardio , as long as you start to get hot , sweaty and out of breath .
while the classic image of cardio be someone huff and puff on a jog , there be so many activity to choose from when it come to cardio : walking and hiking : walking be one of the best cardio exercise out there because it can be do almost anywhere and with little equipment .
all you need be a pair of comfortable , sturdy shoe .
if you be just start out , walk 5 - 10 minute per day and work your way up to 30 minute or more per day .
regular walking can help you lose weight , prevent disease , strengthen bone and muscle , and improve your mood .
hike allows you to explore and enjoy nature , and often burn more calorie than walk by involve steep , more uneven path .
plus , research show just be outside can offer a range of health benefit .
run : like walk , you just need a pair of well - fitting shoe to start running .
no matter where you run or how fast you go , regular run can improve your cardiovascular health , your bone and muscle , and your mental health .
dancing : for a fun , excite workout , try dancing .
while dance can bring the same cardiovascular benefit as other form of cardio , it can also help increase flexibility as you move your body in new way .
and the social aspect of dancing , not to mention learn the choreography , strengthen our cognitive function .
cycling : cycling be a great way to target and strengthen your low body while work your heart and lung .
and the task of stay upright on a bicycle , stationary or not , help your balance and posture .

swimming : when you swim , you get all the cardiovascular benefit of aerobic exercise , with none of the impact .

jump rope : nothing get the heart pump like jump rope .

strength training strength training be a great way to build muscle and lose fat .
this type of exercise involve subject your muscle to some form of resistance through lifting and move heavy object or strain against gravity .
there be so many form of strength training base on equipment and how much weight you be lift .
body weight exercise : when you be get start with strength training , exercise that use only your body weight be usually enough for you to start get strong .
pushup , plank , squat , lunge and burpees be all great option .

weight machine : use weight machine allow for more opportunity to practice your weightlift form before you lift unassisted .

free weight : lifting weight be consider a functional exercise , mean it can make you good at daily task like climb the stair , carry grocery bag and clean around the house .

stretch stretch increase and maintain your flexibility , or your body be ability to move in different way without injury .
stretch regularly can help you perform good physically , use your full range of motion and avoid injury .
the best time to stretch be after a workout , when your muscle be warm up from movement , but you can still benefit from stretch at any time .
static stretching : this kind of stretch be achieve through lengthen your muscle as far as they will go without pain , and then hold that position for 15 - 30 second .
there be two type of static stretching , active and passive .
in active stretching , you contract one muscle to allow the opposite muscle to relax .
lie on your back and lift your leg straight up into the air make your thigh muscle contract , while your hamstring can lengthen and stretch .
in passive stretching , you use an external force , like your hand , to help your body stretch .
when you bend your knee and use your hand to hold your foot behind you to stretch your thigh muscle , that be a passive stretch .
dynamic stretching : before a workout , try dynamic stretch to get your muscle warm up and ready for activity .
dynamic stretching be more active than just touch your toe .
movement include toe touch , high knee , butt kick and lateral shuffle .
if you experience pain when stretching , talk to your doctor or a physical therapist .
they can suggest stretch that will not hurt and will help you increase flexibility slowly .
balance exercise keep your balance be an essential skill in multiple sport and daily activity , and it only get more important as you get old .

in do so , you release tight muscle and strengthen those essential stabilizer muscle , both of which low your risk of fall .
tai chi : a low - impact exercise that can be do almost anywhere , tai chi be an excellent way to control stress and improve balance .
the flow movement from one pose to the next allow you to practice shift your weight from one foot to another with your arm outstretched .

it can help to improve your health and reduce the risk of heart disease and stroke .
speak to a gp first if you have not exercise for some time , or if you have medical condition or concern .
make sure your activity and its intensity be appropriate for your fitness .
adult age 65 and over should : aim to be physically active every day , even if it be just light activity do activity that improve strength , balance and flexibility on at least 2 day a week do at least 150 minute of moderate intensity activity a week or 75 minute of vigorous intensity activity if you be already active , or a combination of both reduce time spend sit or lie down and break up long period of not move with some activity if you have fall or be worry about fall , do exercise to improve your strength , balance and flexibility will help make you strong and feel more confident on your foot .
what count as light activity ?
light activity be move rather than sit or lie down .
example of light activity include : get up to make a cup of tea move around your home walking at a slow pace cleaning and dust vacuum make the bed stand up what count as moderate intensity activity ?
moderate intensity activity will raise your heart rate , and make you breathe faster and feel warmer .
one way to tell if you be work at a moderate intensity level be if you can still talk , but not sing .
example of moderate intensity activity include : walk for health water aerobics rid a bike dance for fitness double tennis push a lawn mower hike try our fitness studio exercise video .
what count as vigorous intensity activity ?
vigorous intensity activity make you breathe hard and fast .
if you be work at this level , you will not be able to say more than a few word without pause for breath .
in general , 75 minute of vigorous intensity activity can give similar health benefit to 150 minute of moderate intensity activity .
most moderate intensity activity can become vigorous if you increase your effort .
example of vigorous activity include : run aerobics swim rid a bike fast or on hill single tennis football hiking uphill dance for fitness martial art try our fitness studio exercise video .
what activity strengthen muscle ?
to get health benefit from strength exercise , you should do them to the point where you need a short rest before repeat the activity .
there be many way you can strengthen your muscle , whether you be at home or in a gym .
example of muscle - strengthening activity include : carry heavy shopping bag yoga pilate tai chi lift weight work with resistance band do exercise that use your own body weight , such as push - ups and sit - ups heavy gardening , such as digging and shovel try exercise routine , include : strength and flexibility exercise sit exercise strength exercise flexibility exercise balance exercise you can do activity that strengthen your muscle on the same or different day as your aerobic activity – whatever be best for you .
muscle - strengthening exercise be not always an aerobic activity , so you will need to do them in addition to your 150 minute of aerobic activity .

this total body workout be a great way for old adult to get start with strength training .

old man and woman work out why you need strength training strength training can help improve overall health and longevity .
it be one of the best way to keep your muscle strong and can preserve independence and energy as you age .
its benefit include:2 build and maintain strength maintain bone density improve balance and coordination improve mobility reduces risk of fall maintain ability to perform everyday activity strength training also require minimal time commitment , make it a great option to fit into your schedule .
get start the key to start weight training , if you be new to it or it be be a long time , be to gradually ease into lift weights.3 lift weight can cause soreness , which be normal , but it should not cause too much pain or discomfort .
see your healthcare provider before try this workout if you have any pain , injury or other health condition .
take your time with the move and only add weight or resistance when you feel comfortable with the exercise .
equipment need various weighted dumbbell , resistance band , a medicine ball , a chair , and a step or staircase .
workout basic begin with a 5- to 10 - minute warm - up of light cardio , such as walk in place .
when you first start , perform each exercise for one set , use no weight or light weight .
weight be suggest for each exercise , but choose your weight accord to your fitness level and goal .
focus on your form before add weight .
to progress , add a set each week until you be do a total of three set of each exercise with 30 second of rest in between each set .
do this workout one or two nonconsecutive day a week , take at least one day of rest between workout .
if you do feel very sore , give yourself extra rest day as need and back off during the next workout .
< END > a squat be a movement we do all day , get up and down from chair , in and out of car , and more .
practice this move with good form will help you build strength in the hip , glute , and thigh .
stand in front of a chair with foot about shoulder - width apart .
bend the knee .
send the hip back and the arm straight out in front of you to balance .
sit all the way down .
as soon as you make contact with the chair , stand back up .
try to stand up without rock back or use momentum .
instead , put the weight on your heel and push into the floor to stand up .
perform 12 reps. modification easier : place your hand on your thigh for support , or position your chair next to a rail if you need more support in stand up .
harder : hold weight in your hand for added intensity .
knee lift with med ball knee lift with a medicine ball this move be great for work on upper body endurance as well as balance and stability .
hold a light weight or medicine ball ( 2 to 5 pound ) in both hand , straight up over your head .
lift the right knee up to waist level while bring the arm down , touch the weight or the ball to the knee .
low the right knee and take the ball all the way back up overhead .
now lift the left knee to hip level , bring the ball down to the knee .
return to start and repeat , alternate side .
continue for 30 to 60 second .
if you have back or knee problem , you may want to avoid the upper body portion of the move and just do the knee lift .
modification easier : use no weight , or hold the weight at chest level as you lift the knee .
harder : speed the movement up , while still maintain control of the weight and your body .
lift the knee as high as you can .
side leg lift side leg lift this move improve your balance as well as strengthen both leg .
the stand leg have to use more stabilizer muscle to keep you balance , while you build strength in the hip and glute with the lift leg .
stand sideways to a chair or wall for support and wrap a resistance band around your ankle ( optional ) .
or you can use light ankle weight ( 1 to 5 pound ) .
shift the weight into the right leg and lift the left leg out to the side , foot flexed and hip , knee and foot in alignment and foot parallel .
try to lift the leg without tilt at the torso .
hold the torso upright as you lift the leg a few inch off the ground .
low back down .
do 12 rep on each leg .
lat pull with band lat pull this move strengthen the lat muscle on either side of the back .
you use these muscle for pull movement like open door or pick thing up .
stand or sit , hold a resistance band over your head with both hand .
your hand should be wide than shoulder - width so that there be tension on the band .
you may need to adjust your hand to change the tension .
make sure your back be flat and your ab be engage .
keep the left hand in place and contract the muscle on the right side of your back to pull the elbow down towards the rib cage .
press back up .
do 12 rep on the right side .
switch side and do 12 rep on the left side .
bicep curl kettlebell curl this exercise strengthen your biceps , muscle that you use every day when you carry thing , open door , or pick thing up .
stand with foot about hip - width apart and hold dumbbell in each hand ( 5 to 8 pound for woman , 8 to 15 pound for men ) .
alternatively , you can use a kettlebell as show .
with your palm face out , contract the biceps and curl the weight up towards your shoulder .
try not to move the elbow as you curl the weight up .
low the weight back down , but keep a slight bend in the elbow at the bottom .
do not swing the weight .
keep the elbow static as you curl the weight .
do 12 reps. tricep extension medicine ball triceps extension the triceps work hard every time you do any kind of push movement , so you want both side of the arm to be strong and balance .
sit or stand , hold a medicine ball or a weight in both hand ( 4 to 10 pound for woman , 8 to 15 pound for men ) .
take the weight straight up overhead , with your arm straight and next to the ear .
slowly bend your elbow , take the weight back behind the head until your elbow be at about a 90 - degree angle .
squeeze the arm to pull the weight back to start without lock the elbow .
do 12 rep , keep the back straight and the ab in .
bird dog this move strengthen the ab as well as the low back and glute .
if your knee hurt or you ca not kneel , try the move lie flat on the floor .
begin on your hand and knee with your back straight and the ab pull in .
lift the right arm up until it be level with the body and , at the same time , lift the left leg up and straighten it until it be parallel to the floor .
hold for several second , low and repeat on the other side , this time lift the left arm and right leg .
continue alternate side for 12 reps. modification easier : lift the arm and leg separately .
harder : add ankle weight and/or hold a small weight in your hand while lift the arm .
ball tap this move be great for the core as well as for balance and stability .
sit in a chair and place a ball in front of both foot .
this can be any kind of small ball or even a large book or some other object if you do not have a ball .
sit straight up .
try not to rest against the back of the chair .
keep your back straight and your ab contract .
place your hand behind your head ( optional ) .
lift your right foot and tap the top of the ball .
take it back down to the floor .
switch side and do the same with your left foot .
repeat for 30 to 60 second , alternate each foot for all repetition .
step - up this exercise strengthen the muscle that support the knee .
if you have knee problem or this bother you , you might want to skip this exercise .
you can do this exercise on a staircase with rail , or on a workout step if you have one .
if you be on a staircase , stand at the bottom step and step up with your right foot .
bring your left foot up onto the stair next to your right and then step it back down on the floor ( hold onto a rail if you need to ) .
keep your right foot on the step the entire time as you step up and down with the left foot .
do 12 rep on that foot and then switch , keep your left foot on the step as you step up with the right leg .
do 1 set of 12 rep on each leg .
hamstring curl this move work the back of the leg , muscle that also support the knee .
you can also use ankle weight instead of a resistance band .
stand in front of a chair and hold onto it for balance if you need to .
loop a resistance band around your ankle ( optional ) , keep it loop under the stand foot .
bend your right knee , bring your foot up behind you , kind of like you be kick your own butt .
keep the right knee point towards the floor and right next to your left knee .
slowly low back down .
do 12 rep on each leg .
incline push - up push - ups work the upper body and this version allow you to gradually ease into push - ups use a wall rather than do them on the floor .
stand a few foot away from a wall or stair rail and tilt slightly forward , back flat and ab in .
place the hand on the wall at chest level , wide than the shoulder .
pull the ab in .
keep the back straight , bend elbow and low body towards the wall until elbow be at 90 - degree angle .
push back to start and repeat .
the farther away from the wall you be , the hard the exercise .
make sure you do not sag in the middle .
keep the ab tight and the back flat .
do 12 reps. chest squeeze with med ball this exercise strengthen the upper body , include the chest and arm .
sit on a chair , back straight and abs in .
hold a medicine ball or weight ( 4 to 6 pound ) at chest level .
hold the weight so that the elbow be bent and out to the side and you be put even tension on the ball with both hand , squeeze the chest .
hold that tension , slowly push the ball straight out in front of you at chest level until the elbow be straight .
continue keep tension on the ball .
it should feel harder the farther out you go .
bend the elbow and pull the ball back to your chest .
do 12 reps. lateral raise this exercise work the shoulder muscle that you use every time you lift something or put something up on a shelf .
stand with foot hip - width apart and hold weight in both hand at your side ( 3 to 8 pound for woman , 5 to 12 pound for men ) .
keep a slight bend in the elbow and the wrist straight , lift the arm up to the side .
stop at shoulder level with palm face the floor .
low back down .
do 12 reps. seat rotation seat rotation work all of the muscle of the torso , include the ab and back .
sit tall on a chair and hold a medicine ball or weight ( 5 to 8 pound for woman , 8 to 15 pound for men ) .
hold the weight at chest level , with shoulder relax and elbow out to the side .
keep the hip and knee face forward , rotate the torso to the right as far as you comfortably can .
focus on squeeze the muscle around your waist .
rotate back to center and then to the left , keep the movement slow and control .
continue alternate side for 12 reps. one rep be a twist to both the right and leave .
safety tip and precaution if you have any health condition , it be important to talk to your healthcare provider before you begin strength training so that you be aware of any individual precaution .
start slow and give yourself plenty of break between exercise .
remember to breathe throughout the move and back off if you experience any pain .
there be also some time when it be important to take a break and check in with your healthcare provider before continue with strength training .
this includes:2 you feel ill and/or have a cold , flu , or infection with a fever you have a swollen or painful muscle or joint you experience significantly more fatigue than usual you feel dizzy or struggle to maintain your balance as long as you communicate with your healthcare provider and take a break if something feel off , you should be able to use strength training to improve your health and reap its many benefit as you age .

hold for 10 second and release .
chest stretch begin seat with relaxed shoulder .
pull extend arm back while grab one hand , keep both hand down near the buttock .
pull your shoulder back and hold for 10 second and release .
seat - and - reach- & -neck- & -inner - thigh - stretch sit and reach stretch sit and reach stretch example sit at the edge of a chair and extend your leg forward with your knee slightly bend .
keep your heel on the floor and toe point toward the ceiling .
extend both arm in front and reach to touch your toe , while slowly bend at the waist without bounce .
hold for 10 second then return to rest position .
neck stretch begin seat and slowly tilt your head to your right shoulder .
hold this position and extend your left arm to the side and downward at waist level .
release , then repeat on the left side .
repeat twice on each side .

slowly lean to your left side by bend your left knee while keep your right leg straight .
keep your left knee from pass your toe .
hold for 10 second then return to rest position and repeat on the right .

circle your shoulder 15 time forward , then 15 time backwards .
hand stretch begin seat with hand reach out in front of you , palm face down .
open both hand to spread your finger apart , then close your hand .
repeat 10 time .

repeat with other side .

seat shin strengthener begin seat on the edge of a chair with leg extend , heel on the floor and knee slightly bend .

do 15 repetition , relax , then do 15 more repetition .
hold the back of a chair .
stand with leg slightly wide than shoulder - width , while point toe outward slightly .
bend your knee slowly , use 2 full second to lower yourself .
adjust leg position if need to keep leg far enough apart so the knee do not pass your toe as you bend .

perform another set , do as many as you can do in good form .
tummy twist tummy twist begin seat , hold a ball with hand close to your stomach and elbow slightly bent .

return to the center and repeat on the left .

core exercise for senior leg lift and bicycle kick leg lifts lie on your back with legs flat against the ground and foot relax .
contract your abdominal muscle while raise one leg 5 inch off the floor and hold for 3 second .
low and repeat on your other leg .
repeat 5 time each side .
bicycle lie on your back with your hand behind your head .
bend your knee and lift your foot so your calf be parallel to the floor .
while draw in your belly button and exhaling , bring one knee to your chest while reach for it with your elbow on the opposite side .
it should look almost as if you be pedal a bicycle .
repeat on the side , and continue with repetition for 30 second .
rest for one minute , and repeat with another 30 - second set .
seat twist sit on an exercise ball , a bosu ball or a roman chair .
if use a ball , begin by place your foot flat on the ground .
if use a roman chair , begin by tuck your leg under the leg support .
bend your torso to a 45 - degree angle from the floor .
place your arm across your chest and lean back as far as you can .
then move forward and slowly twist to the left then lean back again slowly to the start position .
repeat on the right side .
do three set of 15 rep each .
side bend sit on a chair with your foot flat on the floor .
place one hand behind your head and the other arm stretch out to one side .
lean over to the side as if reach toward the floor .
contract your oblique and return to the start position , while keep your chest from fall forward and keep your foot flat on the floor .
repeat five time on each side .
seat knee lift begin seat on a floor mat or a bench .
slowly draw both of your knee towards your chest they touch your chest or until your leg touch your ab .
perform 15 to 20 repetition for one set , and complete three set total .
v. cardio and low - impact exercise for senior speed drill - step ups and water aerobics speed drill draw a ladder design on the floor with chalk or tape .
walk through the step of the ladder by put one foot in a square , then bring the other foot into the same square .
move to the next square and continue until you reach the end of the ladder .
turn around and repeat .
step - ups begin at the bottom of a set of stair .
step on the first stair with your left foot .
then , lift your right foot off the floor and hold it in the air for one second .
step down with your right leg , then the left .
repeat on the opposite side and repeat 10 time per side .
water aerobics keep impact low on the body during exercise may be require by some for many reason include arthritis and joint pain .
for this reason , water aerobics have become a popular choice form of exercise for senior .
it be a safe and effective way to get a workout for the entire body without traditional weight .
water aerobics help build strength and endurance and since most class be take in shallow water , even senior who do not know how to swim can participate .
gym and community pool usually provide these class .
some popular water aerobic exercise include aqua jogging , leg lift , include various balance and strength builder .
biking and tai chi biking & elliptical for a low - impact workout , consider bicycling and the elliptical machine .
these may not be the first exercise to come to mind for low - impact exercise , but they be effective option since they transfer minimal shock to your joint and your body .
both exercise be easy on your joint and body in term of impact .
cycle on the road and on a stationary bike be both viable option for a low - impact workout .
if cycling on the road , you can use an electric bicycle for exercise and also as an effective form of commute .
the assistance from the motor help through tough terrain and make hill easier , allow to make it even easier on your back and neck , a recumbent bicycle be a good alternative as well .
while it might not seem like a low - impact exercise , cycling be actually very easy on the joint since your body absorbs minimal shock from pedal .
you can ride a stationary bike at the gym or invest in a road bike to pedal around your neighborhood .
if an upright bicycle be too hard on your back , neck and shoulder , try a recumbent bike instead .
unlike an upright bike , where you be bent over the handlebar , a recumbent bike allow you to sit back with the pedal and handlebar right in front of you .
tai chi the fact that most tai chi practitioner begin after the age of 50 be a clear sign that it be a good form of exercise for senior .
tai chi be type of meditative exercise that focus on slow , low - impact movement , and breathe technique .
tai chi have be show to improve balance , strength , and flexibility while remain gentle on the joint .
its routine be adaptable to your skill level and you do not need any kind of equipment to start practicing , so it be easy for anyone to get start .
as you advance , tai chi routine and form can get advanced , keep you challenge , and work out your cardiovascular system at the same time .

slowly bend your wrist up and down , then repeat 10 time .
switch side , and perform 10 rep with your other hand .
repeat one more set of 10 on each side .

bend your arm at the elbow to lift the dumbbell ¾ of the way to your shoulder , without move your elbow away from your side .
do 10 to 12 repetition per arm .
upright row upright front row begin stand with your foot shoulder - width apart , knee slightly bent , and partially lean forward .
hold one dumbbell in each hand in front of you , with palm face toward your body .
lift both dumbbell toward your chin while keep your back straight and shoulder stationary .
return to start position and repeat 10 time .
knee extension begin seat in a chair with your back straight and knee bent .

repeat with your left leg .
