< END > < START > 1. ease into the first few week of training i find beginner be ready to crush themselves in their very first workout .
in other word , go too hard , which be not advise .
i recommend that lifter ease into their workout by stop just shy of all - out failure on all exercise , at least for the first two week .
this do not mean you be not train hard , it mean that you be give your body the chance to adjust to the extra stimulus .
the reality be as a beginner you be literally start from nothing .
you can do very basic exercise , with moderate to hard effort , and get good result .
while those beginner gain will last only a few month , it be important not to go too aggressive as it will not help you get anywhere faster .
in fact , it may derail you right out of the gate due to injury , excessive soreness , and the inability to work out multiple time a week because you be too “ beat up ” .
2. focus on complete at least 12 workout in the first 30 day i give all my new client a goal of work out 12 time in their first month .
if they can master carve out time to get 12 workout in ( on average 3 per week ) over a 30 - day period , they will have make the necessary behavior change to stick with go to the gym long - term .
get start as a beginner can be tough , as you need to create a new lifestyle routine to accommodate you go to the gym , work out , and then come home .
if you also have to do that before or after work , you will need to pack a bag and some meal .
like any habit , work out be all about repetition and make consistent practice .
12 workout in 30 day not only provide the muscle with enough stimulus to get strong , but it give you the opportunity to create a whole new system on how to allocate your time .
3. choose 5 - 6 total exercise to do each day i suggest that every beginner find a program that have them do no more than 6 exercise on a single day .
ideally , you would be choose 2 - 4 compound exercise , and another 2 - 3 isolation - type movement to build out a good workout program .
as a beginner , it can be tempt to do every exercise you see on social medium on a single day .
you be constantly bombard by “ new cut - edge workout and exercise ” .
if you train more than 3 day a week , you would simply just add more workout during the week , but still , keep the same number of exercise per workout .
check out these workout idea : 3 - day beginner workout program 2 - day beginner workout program 4. keep workout under 1 hour keep workout under 1 hour i recommend beginner get efficient with their workout , i.e .
do a lot of work in a short amount of time .
the idea be to push yourself hard to get a full workout do in an hour .
beginner often struggle with two thing .
the first be be consistent in the gym , often say they do not have enough time to get three or more workout in during the week .
the second be when they be at the gym , they often have less than optimal workout because they be too busy get distract .
both of these can be solve by have a clear workout program that be design for beginner and can be do in under an hour .
this will keep you focused and feel like you be accomplish a lot by the end of the workout .
once you get three workout a week at an hour each , and you be do all your exercise every workout with efficiency , look to add another workout in the week to take your result to the next level .
i suggest you turn your phone to not disturb mode , and switch over to airplane mode so you can not access social medium or email .
the phone be a huge distraction in the gym .
most lifter will rely on their phone for everything : look at their workout program , texting people during workout , surf social medium , and answer email ( or even take call ) .
6. stay off social medium stay off social medium !
we live in a time where everyone be connect on social medium , and the gym be no different .
too often i see people ( not just beginner ) on instagram , tik tok , and facebook mindlessly scroll between set .
this be one of the fast way to lose precious minute in your workout , and not lose focus .
i tell my client that if they have enough time to do mindless thing between set , they have rest long enough .
you should be work hard enough to warrant your rest period , which typically consist of you sit down , catch your breath , shake your muscle , and mentally recover for your next set .
any more than that , and you be just wait time .
7. time your rest period i often find beginner either rest no time at all or rest an eternity between set .
both be wrong .
the reality be , most beginner can get by rest 90 second between set .
this allow you to recover from a tough set , but also keep the stimulus on the muscle enough between set to have a compounding fatigue effect ( basically , over the course of the workout you want the muscle to tire out ) .
while more advanced lifter may need long than 2 minute , most beginner be not strong enough relative to their body mass and ability to warrant a very long rest period like you would see in elite - level powerlifters .
< END > < START > start a fitness journey can be intimidate .
there be workout to learn , diet to follow , willpower to conjure , and self - consciousness to overcome .
but make the decision to start a fitness regimen and make stride toward improve your health be the absolute best thing you can do for yourself — mind and body .. here , eric answer the most common training question he get from people who be start their quest toward fitness .
i do not know how to use the equipment or do any workout .
how do i get start ?
as a complete beginner , the gym can certainly be an intimidating place .
this be why i suggest hire a personal trainer for a good eight to 10 session .
he or she can teach you what muscle group each piece of equipment work , as well as proper exercise technique , breathe pattern , and rep cadence .
a good trainer will also help you develop a workout program that be suit to your present level of fitness , particular goal , and that address any injury or limitation that you may have .
what type of training should i do to lose weight ?
when it come to lose weight , you need a combination of weight / resistance training and cardiovascular exercise .
many people make the error of perform too much cardio and neglect weightlifting , think that only treadmill , stationary bike , and stair stepper be responsible for burn fat — but this be far from true .
while cardio will certainly help you burn extra calorie , it be weight train that be go to stimulate the metabolism ( so that you become a fat - burning machine ) , change the composition of your body , and bring about the shape and contour you want .
i suggest at least three to four day per week lift weight and four to five perform cardio — preferably first thing in the morning or right after resistance training .
person grip a barbell for a romanian deadlift exercise what type of training should i do to build strength and muscle ?
for building strength and muscle , you will need a well - design weight train program that primarily utilize free weight and compound ( multi - joint ) exercise .
a four - day - per - week program work quite well for most , use a two on , one off ; two on , two off pattern .
this allow you to hit each muscle group hard once per week , while provide you three day for rest and recovery ( which be when actual growth take place ) .
i suggest start with about four exercise for three set each for major muscle like back , quad , hamstring , chest , and shoulder .
for small group like biceps , triceps , trap , ab , forearm , and calf , you will do well with just three movement for two to three set each .
perform one to three warmup set before each exercise ( more be need earlier in the workout ) , and then work set of 13 to 15 , 10 to 12 , and 7 to 9 reps. beginner workout how often do i need to work out ?
how often you need to work out depends on your fitness level , goal , and time limitation .
the lofty the goal , the more time you will have to spend go after it .
that say , if you have a very demanding job , a family , or other important personal responsibility , you may not be able to spend hour per week work out .
then you will need to be patient when it come to reach your goal .
to make decent progress you need to hit the gym at least three day per week for an hour at a time .
however , as time pass , you will begin to require more time in order to see continued progress .
i suggest start out with three gym session per week and add to your program every month or so .
how much time should i spend in the gym ?
like the last question , this depend on how fit you currently be , what goal you have set for yourself , and how much time you have to devote to work out .
for some people it may be best to schedule three hour - long workout per week , while others may find it more convenient and beneficial to train five to six day per week — but for only 30 minute .
in other word , it be best to think about how many total hour per week you will spend in the gym , and then decide how best to spread it out .
another important point to consider be quality of time and not just quantity .
someone who be very dedicated and focus on their training can often get far more accomplished in just 30 minute than someone who be there for an hour , but constantly distract by their phone , chat with others , and watch rather than do .
rest how much rest do i need ?
certain exercise be far more demand on the body than others and require more rest between set .
for example , a set of 15 rep of barbell squat will not only tax the thigh , glute , and low back , but will also have you breathe like a freight train .
you may find that you need a good three to four minute before you be ready to get to the next set .
on the other hand , perform 15 dumbbell side lateral may only require 45 to 60 second of recovery time .
another point to consider be what your primary goal be and how weight training will work best to reach it .
someone who be in the gym to build massive size and power will want to rest for long period in between set so as to be able to lift maximum weight for maximum reps. when you be look to burn body fat and increase endurance , it be best to keep heart rate elevate and move quickly from set to set , even if the weight be lighter .
as for between workout , you may find that as a beginner that a full day of rest be need in between weight training session .
however , as you progress and become more resilient , it be possible to train for day without a break , just as long as you never work the same muscle two day in a row .
cardio can be do daily .
should i start a supplement regimen ?
in the beginning of your health and fitness journey , the main focus should be on implement an intelligent and efficient workout regimen and a healthy and balanced nutrition program .
anyone who tell you to immediately jump on all sort of sport supplement be either misinformed or try to make a buck ( well , most of them ) .
after spend eight to 12 solid week in the gym , work hard and consistently while carefully follow a sound diet , it be appropriate to think about add supplement into the mix .
be there really a 30- to 60 - minute window to consume protein post - workout ?
why ?
it be actually true that within the first hour after work out intensely with weight , the body be in a special metabolic state where protein and carbohydrate be partition toward muscle and away from fat cell .
this be because during this period , insulin sensitivity be extremely high , which mean amino acid and carbs will very readily be absorb , assimilate , and store directly into damage muscle cell .
this allow for repair , recovery , and recuperation to start immediately , and over time you will get far good result than eat your post - workout meal outside of this anabolic window .
out of shape training i be severely out of shape .
be there anything that be not safe for me to do ?
while it be likely safe for you to begin a light workout program , preferably under the care of an experienced and educate personal trainer , it would be best for you to consult with your physician before even step into a gym .
get the green light from your doc will give you peace of mind and keep you from needlessly cause yourself harm , illness , or injury , especially when you be take step to improve your health and wellness .
do not be dishearten ; just talk to your doctor first to get a physical and come up with a strategy .

absolutely , yes .
not only be outside activity great for your body , they have be prove to improve your mental wellbeing — depression be often a factor for people who find it difficult to get in shape .
these type of activity be especially great when it come to get in your cardiovascular training .
it be far more enjoyable to hike , dance , bike , run stair , or swim than to walk on a treadmill every session .
body fat caliper how do i know my training be work ?
what performance measure should i be track ?
carefully track your progress be extremely important when embark on any kind of physical fitness program .
if possible , it be a good idea to meet with a coach or trainer every two to four week to have your weight , body fat , and complete measurement take .
you can take it a step far by have regular blood test via your primary physician if you be try to regulate general health measure like total cholesterol , ratio of ldl to hdl , triglyceride , and blood pressure .

obviously if you be look to get big and more muscular , you know you be head in the right direction if your shirt be fit tighter in the arm , chest , and through the back .
the scale be not always a telltale sign of whether your program be yield result , since it be very possible for people , especially woman , to drop several size without lose a single pound .
always remember that muscle weigh more than fat , but it take up far less space .
what do i do when i hit a plateau ?
when stagnation set in , it be time to look carefully at your overall program and decide what change need to be make to kickstart progress once again .
sometimes it be a case of simply add in more work or tweak your diet by add or subtract calorie ( depend on the goal ) .
time you have to ask yourself if you be truly give it 100 percent every day in the gym .
simply show up be not go to get the job do — you need to focus , concentrate , and give your all to every set and rep. another possibility be that your body and mind have adapt to the exercise and type of cardio you have be do and need a change .
try change some of your weight training movement , switch to different cardio machine , use more or less resistance , or alter rest between set .

4. chin - up this pull - up variant have you supinate the hand ( turn them inward ) when pull your chin to the bar .

how to train with bodyweight exercise with weight , you progress by lift more absolute load or the same amount of weight for more reps. you do not have that option for bodyweight movement , so you will have to rely on additional volume above all .
start by find how many rep you can do of a bodyweight exercise before your form really break down .
exercise selection do not try to perform 16 different bodyweight movement per day .
the rule of exercise selection be the same ; cluster movement together to double down on muscular stimulation , or pick one for each body part to train yourself from head to toe .
for example , a low - body calisthenics day could contain squat , walk lunge , and box jump .
set and rep once you have establish your limit , perform multiple set of 3 – 5 rep shy of that limit .
if you can do 12 pull - ups , hit three set of eight .
each week , or workout session , add one to two rep to each set .
once you reach your max rep for all three set , drop the rep count back to your start number and add a set .
you can also alter the tempo of each movement to make the rep more challenging .

draw a card and perform the move associate with that suit for the number of rep on the card ; or 11 rep for face card and 15 for ace .

improve mobility most bodyweight move mimic everyday life .
you squat to get out of a chair ; you lunge when you walk up the stair ; you technically perform a pull - up when close the garage door .
most movement pattern can be break down into six basic category — a vertical pull , vertical push , horizontal pull , horizontal push , knee - base movement , and a hip - base movement .
here be an example of each : horizontal push : push - up horizontal pull : inverted row vertical push : military press vertical pull : pull - up knee - base movement : squat hip - base movement : glute bridge by perform bodyweight exercise , you be improve your proficiency in these pattern and make yourself strong in these position .
barbell work accomplishes this as well , of course , but with the obvious caveat that you must have access to weight in the first place .
unparalleled convenience unlike powerlifters or strongman competitor who need specialized equipment for their training , bodyweight aficionado can go hard just about anywhere .
since you be forgo the barbell for your own body weight , calisthenics - base routine can be perform wherever you have enough physical space .
woman do decline push - up this make bodyweight train convenient in a way that other activity ca not match .

scalable for all level you may think that squat or do a push - up with your bodyweight be the ground floor for all exercise , but that be not the case .

when you be use your body as the weight , you ca not just remove 10 or 20 pound as you can with machine or dumb­bells .
but there be way to modify move to decrease or increase the resistance .
you can adjust your body position — for example , do push - ups against a wall rather than the floor — or you can change the number of time you repeat an exercise or modify the pace you be work at .
it be good for your health literally thousand of study have show that the more you move , the low your risk for heart disease , diabetes , obesity , multiple type of cancer , joint pain , and alzheimer be disease .
exercise can also lift your mood , reduce your stress level , and improve your sleep .
body - weight exercise be no exception .

hammond recommend do four set of each of the exercise below .
if you be a beginner , start with two set of 15 rep and increase the number of set as you get strong .
and if you have an injury or illness that may limit your ability to safely exercise , check with your doctor before start any new workout program .
note : some of these move suggest use a yoga mat .
if you do not have one , try use a folded towel or complete the exercise on carpet to lessen the impact on your hand or knee .
chest 1. push - up push - up start on your hand and knee on a yoga mat on the floor , with your hand rest slightly wide than the width of your shoulder .
straighten your leg out behind you so you be be support by your hand and the ball of your foot .
keep your body in a straight line from the top of your head to your heel ( hold your head up in line with your spine ) .
bend your elbow and low your chest until it nearly touch the mat .
pause and then push yourself back up to the start position .
if that be too difficult , complete the push - up with your knee on the floor .
one set be 12 reps. 2. push - up shuffle push - up - shuffle complete a push - up ( either on your knee or with your leg extend behind you , depend on your fitness level ) .
then , keep your core engage and shuffle your right hand and right foot a step to the right side .
bring your left hand and foot to meet them .
complete another push - up there .
return to center and repeat on the opposite side .
one set be five shuffle in each direction .
3. isometric chest squeeze isometric - chest - squeeze stand with your hand in front of you with a 90 - degree bend in your elbow .
hold your hand together and squeeze your chest as hard as you can .
hold the tension for up to 30 second and release ; that be one rep. relate : should you try a plank and push - up challenge ?
arm 1. triceps dip tricep - dip sit in front of a bench or coffee table or at the end of a couch with your leg extend out in front of you away from the furniture .
position your hand on top of the furniture behind you with your hand about shoulder - width apart and your fingertip point toward your body .
straighten your arm and pull your body up so it be hover over the floor .
then engage your triceps muscle as you bend your elbow until they be at about a 90 - degree angle .

you should be support most of your body be weight in your arm to get the great benefit from the move .
to make the exercise easier , keep your knee bend at a 90 - degree angle .
one set be 12 reps. 2. plank up - and - down plank - up - down get into a plank position on the floor : your hand should be on the mat with your shoulder directly above them , legs extend straight back behind you , toe on the mat , and your body form a straight line from top of head to heel .
( if that be too difficult , you can keep your knee on the floor . )
low your left elbow down to the mat and then low your right elbow down to the mat so you be now in a forearm plank .
keep your core engage and your body in a straight line .
push up and straighten your right arm .
then straighten your left arm as well .
repeat for 30 second , switch off which arm go first ; that be one set .
3. triangle push - ups triangle - pushup settle into a plank position but place your hand close together under your chest and form a triangle with your index finger and your thumb ( your thumb should be in a straight line form the bottom side of the triangle ) .
low your chest toward the floor as if you be do a regular push - up , keep your elbow close to your body .
pause at the bottom and then push off the floor to return to the start position .
modify by complete the push - up with your knee on the floor or by move your hand slightly wide than the triangle shape .
one set be 12 rep back 1. superman y superman - y lie facedown on a mat with your arm extend in a y position overhead and your leg be extend directly behind you on the mat .
use your back and shoulder , lift your chest and arm off the mat .
hold and then low into the starting position .
one set be 15 reps. 2. bird dog bird - dog position yourself on your hand and knee on your mat with hand beneath your shoulder and your knee beneath your hip .
while keep your core engage and stable , raise your right arm straight in front of you and extend your left leg straight out behind you , reach both away from the body at the same time so both be parallel to the floor .
hold , engage the hamstring and glute ; then bring your arm and leg back to center .
repeat with your left arm and right leg .
complete 15 rep on each side for one set .
3. superman t superman - t lie facedown on a mat with your arm extend out to your side so your body be in a t position .
use your back and shoulder , lift your chest and arm off the mat .
hold and then low into the starting position .
one set be 15 reps. relate : more exercise for strengthen your back core and abdominal muscle 1. plank plank start on the mat on your hand and knee with your hand beneath your shoulder .
extend your leg behind you so your toe be press into the floor to stabilize your body .
keep your neck in an unstrained , neutral position with your eye focus on a spot on the floor about a foot in front of you .
you should feel your leg and glute work to hold your body steady .
your body should be form a straight line from the top of your head to your heel .
hold for 30 second , or as long as you can manage ; that be one set .
2. bicycle crunch bicycle - crunch lie on your back with your arm bent and your hand touch the back of your head ( but not fully support it ) .
pull your knee up and into your chest as you lift your shoulder blade off the floor .
extend your right leg straight out in front of you ( make a 45 - degree angle with the floor ) , while simultaneously twist your upper body toward your left knee , so your right elbow be extend toward your left knee .
hold and then repeat in the opposite direction with your left leg extend and your left elbow twist to meet your right knee , for a total of 30 second for one set .
3. side plank side - plank lie on your side with your forearm on the floor at a 90 - degree angle point away from you on the mat ( chest and upper body be lift off the mat ) and your leg extend so your body be in a straight line on the mat .
stack your foot on top of each other and lay your top arm on your waist .
( if that be too difficult , place your upper leg on the floor in front of the low leg . )
lift your hip off the floor while hold your core tight .
your body should form a straight line from top of head to heel .
lift your top arm straight up into the air so it be perpendicular to the floor .
hold for 30 second or more .
to make it more challenging , lift your top leg up and down as you hold the plank .
switch side and repeat ; that be one set .
relate : more exercise for strong ab and a strong core legs 1. jump squat jump - squat stand with your foot shoulder - width apart .
hinge from your hip and bend your knee to lower into a squat position , as if you be sit down in a chair .
keep your weight in your heel and your chest up throughout the movement .
pause at the bottom , then drive through the heel as you jump straight into the air .
land softly on your foot and immediately lower into a squat to repeat .
one set be 10 reps. 2. reverse lunge reverse - lunge from a stand position with foot together , step your right foot directly behind you .
low your hip and drop your right knee so it be bent at a 90 - degree angle and your right heel be off the floor .
as you bend your left knee , it should form a 90 - degree angle , too — and be careful not to let that knee shift far forward than your left foot .
keep your back upright and eye look straight ahead .
squeeze your glute , quad , and calf as you press your left heel into the floor , and bring your right leg forward to return to stand .
do 10 rep and then repeat on the opposite leg ; that be one set .
2. donkey kick donkey - kick start on your mat with your hand and knee on the floor .
tuck your chin slightly into your chest .
keep your core tight and lift your left leg up toward the ceiling , as if you be try to press the bottom of your right foot into the ceiling .
your knee should maintain a 90 - degree bend the whole time .
be careful not to arch your back or shift your hip as you move your leg .
hold , and then bring your leg back down to the start position .
repeat for 12 rep and then switch side ; that be one set .
relate : more leg exercise for glute , quad , and hamstring full body 1. burpee burpee stand with your foot shoulder - width apart .
in one fluid motion , low your body into a squat ( hinge at the hip as if sit in an imaginary chair , hold chest and upper body upright ) , place your hand on the floor in front of your foot and jump your foot back so you land in a plank position .
then , jump your foot back to where they be near your hand and complete a powerful jump straight into the air .
to make it more challenging , add a push - up before jump up from the plank .
if you be a beginner , stand up after jump out of the plank position ( eliminate the jump into the air at the end ) .
one set be 10 reps. 2. mountain climber mountain - climber start in a plank position .
engage your core as you lift your right leg slightly off the floor and bring your right knee toward the center of your chest .
return the right leg back to plank position as you switch side , draw your left knee into your chest .
continue switch back and forth at a quick pace for 30 second ; that be one set .
3. bear crawl bear - crawls start on the floor with your hand and knee on the mat , keep your back flat and your wrist beneath your shoulder .
lift your knee off the floor about an inch so your weight be be support by your hand and toe .
at the same time , step your right hand and leave foot forward while stay close to the floor .
then move your left hand and right foot forward .
repeat up the length of the mat and then reverse direction ( up and back down your mat be one rep ) , ideally for 20 rep ; that be one set .

1. bar muscle - ups muscle up best for : strength | challenge : high hang from a pullup bar and then swing your body forward a bit , pull your shoulder blades together so your head and chest move forward .

you may need to practice the motion .

you will feel as if you be cheat a regular pullup .

low yourself back down and reset for the next rep. 2. pullups man do pullup at a gym best for : strength | challenge : medium grab onto a bar and hang so that your arm be straight and your foot be not touch the ground .

< END > < START > if you be on the hunt for bodyweight exercise that you can do from anywhere ( read : the comfort of your own home ) , then you be in the right place .
we be big fan of simple yet effective home workout here at uk - most of us be time short as be , so hour - long weight training workout that require a drive to the gym just will not be doable .
a 20 - minute session you can do from your living room , however , be a whole different matter .
you can squeeze in before the kid wake up or when you get home from work , in your pyjama or favourite gym kit - whatever float your boat .
that say , many wonder whether bodyweight exercise be actually effective or worth your time .
for those of you who do not know , the basic definition of a bodyweight exercise be a workout move you do use just the weight of your body - think a push - up , squat , or lunge .
bodyweight workout utilize resistance so as to create muscle tension , in turn boost both your strength level and general fitness .
accord to , the fit woman in the uk , pt and crossfit coach , there be load of benefit of do workout simply use your bodyweight .
`` be able to control your own weight can involve great strength and be a fantastic way to build muscle as well as grow your body awareness , `` she explain .
`` just look at gymnast - they largely use their own body weight and be incredibly strong .
`` benefit include improved fitness , strength and muscle mass , good blood flow , plus they put less strain on your joint if you be recover from injury .
`` bodyweight training also allow you to build a strong base with a variety of exercise that can be make more challenging by rep , tempo and incline , `` campbell continue .
to improve your fitness week on week , campbell and , gym manager , coach and personal trainer at wit house london , recommend aim for progressive overload - that be , gradually increase the amount of rep or set of an exercise you do so your body adapts and get strong .
`` as long as you be consistent with the movement and your session , you could see result within a month , `` campbell share .
for their top pick of the best move to try at home , keep scrolling .
look for other workout to try ?
this pilates workout get our vote .
bodyweight exercise : 10 best to try anytime , anywhere 1. air squat accord to campbell , air squat be a great bodyweight move to try at home .
`` it be a multi - purpose movement in that it can be use to warm up and mobilise your body before lift weight , perform in volume to build leg endurance , or do as part of a recovery routine by promote blood flow to your leg and glute .
`` he agree , add that they be a great low body movement to improve mobility of your ankle , knee and hip and also leg strength .
how to : imagine you be sit on a chair , with your hip go back and your knee forward .
keep your chest up , keep sit down until your hip be ideally below the parallel line of your knee .
then stand up .
sometimes raise your arm to eye level as you descend can help to maintain your chest position in this movement , so try that if you find you be lean forward too much .
how long : start with 5 round of 20 air squat .
when you be use to that , try add time under tension , advise campbell - aim to take 4 second to get from stand to the bottom of the squat , as a start point .
2. lunge next up ?
the humble lunge .
often overlook , this bodyweight exercise have a multitude of benefit and can be perform in a variety of way , share the expert .
`` they work your stability and balance as well as require the single leg strength to drive from the bottom position , `` share campbell .
how to : bring one leg out in front of you , and as your foot land on the floor lower down your back knee to touch the floor with your front leg create a right angle .
drive back up from the front leg to standing .
how long : start with 5 round of 20 and build from there .
3. jumping lunge jump lunge , accord to campbell , be great for explosive strength and building leg endurance via lactate threshold training ( aka when lactate acid build up in your blood faster than the body can remove it ) .
`` this mean you will be able to work for long and at a high intensity , `` she explain .
how to : perform as a regular lunge - as above - but instead of step into each position , jump explosively .
how long : build up with a few set of 10 to 16 reps. 4. push up a push up be one of the best shoulder exercise you can do , plus the most basic form of push strength .
`` it can also be easily scale to suit all ability , `` share campbell .
how to : begin in a top plank position with your hand underneath your shoulder and low your chest down to the floor whilst maintain the same body position .
once your chest have touch the floor , push yourself back up to your start position .
this can be scale to lower yourself down to a bench or box – this be preferable to a kneeling push up as it include the full range of motion and maintain the core demand of the movement .
how long : to build strength with these you want to aim for progressive overload where you increase the rep or set you perform each session .
for example , one week you could perform 3 set of 6 to 8 , then the next week , aim for 3 set of 8 to 10. either way , your workload be increase and your body be therefore work harder and will need to adapt to get strong .
5. ring row this be another great movement that can be easily adapt to make it challenge for people of all ability .
`` they be incredibly underrated and a great way to build lat and back strength , too , `` share campbell .
how to : with your foot on the floor , either the full foot for more support or just heel to make it hard , begin with your arm fully extend and lat engage by pull your shoulder blade back and down .
pull the ring in to touch your chest and low back to the start position in a controlled manner .
to make it more difficult , make your body more horizontal or elevate your foot on a box or bench .
how long : like push ups , you want to build rep week on week where you push yourself a bit more each session .
aim for 3 set of 6 to 8 and progress from there .
try add a pause at the top or a tempo on the way down for ultimate bang for your buck .
6. pull up a pull up be another seriously simple yet effective bodyweight move - it be one of the most pure and simple form of strength and further motivates so many woman to get strong in the mission to get a pull up .
again , unless you have a sturdy enough piece of kit at home , do try this one at the gym , too .
how to : start with your arm fully extend hang from a bar and initiate the movement by squeeze your shoulder blades together to avoid overly use your trap .
pull up until your chin be above the bar , squeeze your leg together throughout the rep. low yourself down in a controlled manner to your start position .
how long : if you can perform one rep or less , practise negative pull ups so you be able to eventually do more .
`` this mean that you jump to the top of the pull up position and control the descent , `` explain the expert .
if you can perform at least two rep , she advise gradually add rep or set on each session .
7. wall walk wall walk be a simple movement but simultaneously very humble and deceive , share campbell .
it be a great way of build shoulder strength in a way that be a bit different , plus it be slightly more fun than other movement , she reckons .
how to : start with your body face down on the ground with your hand by your shoulder and foot touch the wall .
push back into a down dog position before place your foot on the wall and then move your hand and foot at the same time up the wall until your hand be a couple of inch away from the wall and body in one line .
low yourself back to your start position in a controlled manner .
to scale these , perform with your foot on a box or bench and stop when your hand be underneath your hip .
how long : to build up your capacity add in more rep or set each time you perform them .
start by aim for 3 set of 6 to 8 .
8. sit ups top tip : fold a towel up and place it under your low back for support and full range of motion .
how to : start by lie down on your back with your foot flat against the floor and your knee bent .
with hand on either side of your body , brace your core and raise your upper body off the floor , sit up towards your knee until you be upright .
then , brace your core again and be careful not to strain your neck , low yourself back towards the ground .
repeat .
how long : aim for 3 set of 6 to 8 reps. 9. plank you will all have hear of a plank , but for good reason - accord to the trainer , it be a great move for core stability which will transfer over to other move , such as squat and deadlifts , and also improve your posture .
how to : start with your elbow , forearm , and toe on the floor so you be hold your body in a straight line .
keep your core tight , your spine neutral and your shoulder brace , hold the position , remember to breathe .
how long : aim for 3 set of 45 to 60 second .
10. burpees last but by no mean least , another bodyweight move you will have heard of be a burpee - a high intensity interval train move that will get your heart rate up and boost your cardio .
how to : start by stand with your foot beneath your hip , arm by your side .
lower yourself into your standard squat position , put both hand on the floor and jump your leg back into a plank position .
brace your core , bring yourself back up to your start position and repeat .
how long : aim for 3 set of 12 to 15 reps. what happen if i only do bodyweight exercise ?
as campbell explains , bodyweight exercise - such as air squat or lunge - be good to incorporate in lighter or active recovery session .
`` many athlete include them in their training programme and study have prove can massively benefit your training , `` she share .
`` perform at the correct intensity for each individual , they will promote blood flow to the muscle help to speed up recovery without put them under too much strain with added load from a weight , `` she continue .
additionally , the muscle time under tension can easily be manipulate in these exercise through alteration in the tempo of the movement , or by add pause .
in short , bodyweight exercise be a great way for beginner to build both muscle and strength .

do resistance band work for build muscle ?
in short , yes , resistance band be effective for build muscle .
“ the key to help your muscle grow be tension , sufficient recovery , muscle adaptation , and progressive load , ” say , all of which be feasible through use resistance band alone .
that say : if you be an * avid * user of resistance band ( like , you be band up every single day ) , know that in the future you will need to up the ante : “ your body will eventually get use to these band , even the heavy one , and you will want to incorporate weight to further enhance your strength , ” say .
it be all a part of continue to progress your weight load and challenge your bod .
for example , you can do move like deadlifts , squat , and glute bridge with both a resistance band and a dumbbell to give your workout that extra difficulty of tension — result in more room for muscle building .

how to choose the right resistance band resistance band come in many form and be use for various type of workout , include physical therapy , pre - workout mobility warmups , strengthen muscle , speed and agility drill , and stretch .
there be a few different type of resistance band you can choose from , depend on your goal .
some look like a long , round tube with handle at each end , while others that take the shape of a shorter close loop .
resistance band that be longer with handle can be use for more upper body and full body workout , whereas the shorter close loop resistance band be best for leg , glute , and low body , say .
resistance band be inexpensive compare to machine and require little storage space , make them a great option to have on standby .
he recommend incorporate resistance band exercise 2 - 3 time a week in conjunction with weight and different form of cardio , like walking or swimming .
how do resistance band work ?
when you use a resistance band , it stretch to create tension , and your muscle have to overcome this oppositional force .
in do so , your muscle work harder , result in strong , more defined muscle .
“ you can add them to weight bar to increase the resistance , and they help you improve range of motion when weight stop work because of gravity .
” they can also be your gym buddy when you want to go deeply into an exercise or stretch .
“ when stretching , resistance band can take the place of another person to extend your reach and provide pressure , ” say .
“ they also require more core activation for most move .
” resistance band be also a safe way to fight osteoporosis and increase bone density .
“ there be less force on the joint , so if you be recover from an injury or have joint pain , these can be your best friend , ” say .
this make them great for beginner .
“ resistance band be versatile and can be use for many muscle group while be easy on the joint .
everyone from beginner to bodybuilder can use them effectively .

11. pushup foundational but not a cinch , pushup require upper body strength , yes , but also core and low - body stabilization .

push up and repeat for 12 reps. switch leg and repeat .

< END > < START > there be pretty much no science behind the cool - down advice .
the cool - down , doctor say , “ be an understudied topic .
” ” everyone think it be an establish fact , ” he add , “ so they do not study it .
” it be not even clear what a cool - down be suppose to be .
some say you just have to keep move for a few minute  walk to your car after you finish a run rather than stop abruptly and stand there .
others say you have to spend 5 to 10 minute do the same exercise , only slowly .
after your run , then transition into a walk .
still others say that a cool - down should include stretch .
and it be not clear what the cool - down be suppose to do .
some say it alleviate muscle soreness .
others say it prevent muscle tightness or relief strain on the heart .
exercise researcher say there be only one agree - on fact about the possible risk of suddenly stop intense exercise .
when you exercise hard , the blood vessel in your leg be expand to send more blood to your leg and foot .
and your heart be pump fast .
if you suddenly stop , your heart slow down , your blood be pool in your leg and foot , and you can feel dizzy , even pass out .
the best athlete be most vulnerable , say doctor , a cardiologist and marathon runner who be an exercise researcher at hartford hospital in connecticut .
“ if you be well trained , your heart rate be slow already , and it slow down even faster with exercise , ” he say .
“ also , there be big vein with a large capacity to pool blood in your leg .
” that effect can also be deleterious for someone with heart disease .
“ that be always a concern , ” doctor say .
“ but to my knowledge there be not a wealth of experimental data .
” but do it matter for the ordinary , average athlete ?
“ probably not a great deal , ” doctor say .
and , anyway , most people do not just stand there , stock still , when their workout be over .
they walk to the locker room or to their house or car , get the cool - down benefit without officially “ cool down .
” the idea of the cool - down seem to have originate with a popular theory  now know to be wrong  that muscle become sore after exercise because they accumulate lactic acid .
in fact , lactic acid be a fuel .
it be good to generate lactic acid , it be a normal part of exercise , and it have nothing to do with muscle soreness .
but the lactic acid theory lead to the notion that by slowly reduce the intensity of your workout you can give lactic acid a chance to dissipate .
yet , doctor say , even though scientist know the lactic acid theory be wrong , it remain entrench in the public be mind .
“ it be an idea we ca not get rid of , ” he say .
in fact , doctor say , one study of cyclist conclude that because lactic acid be good , it be well not to cool down after intense exercise .
lactic acid be turn back into glycogen , a muscle fuel , when cyclist simply stop .
when they cool down , it be waste , use up to fuel their muscle .
as far as muscle soreness go , cool down do not do anything to alleviate it , doctor say .
and there be no physiological reason why it should .
that be also the conclusion of a study of muscle soreness by south african researcher who ask 52 healthy adult to walk backward downhill on a treadmill for 30 minute  an exercise that can cause sore leg muscle .
the participant be randomly assign to cool down by walk slowly uphill for 10 minute or simply to stop exercising .
the result , the researcher report , be that cool down do nothing to prevent sore muscle .
and muscle tightness ?
“ in a different generation we would have call it an old wife tale , ” doctor say .
“ now i guess i would call it an old physiologist tale .
there be no data to support the idea that a cool - down help .
” but , he add , once again , “ it be an idea we ca not get rid of .
” exercise researcher say they act on their own advice .
doctor say if he be do a really hard track workout he will jog for a short distance when he finish to avoid become dizzy .
if he run a half marathon , he will “ start shuffle forward , ” after he cross the finish line , for the same reason .
as for doctor , he do not cool down at all .
he be a soccer player and , he say , he see no particular reason to do anything after exercise other than just stop .

incline bench press a. grab a pair of dumbbell and lie on your back on a bench set to a low incline ( 15 to 30 degree ) .
lift the dumbbell up to arm be length so they be over your chin , and hold them with your palm turn toward your foot ( thumb face each other ) .
b. slowly low the weight to your upper chest , pause , and push them back up over your chin .
rep : 10 to 12 one - arm snatch a. hold a dumbbell in your right hand use an overhand grip .
with your foot shoulder - width apart , bend your knee and place the dumbbell on the floor .
b. perform a high pull : in one explosive movement , straighten your leg and hip while bend your elbow to pull the dumbbell upward .
c. at the dumbbell be high point , drop your hip and “ catch ” the weight by rotate your wrist under the dumbbell .
quickly straighten your arm so the dumbbell be now over the top of your shoulder .
complete all your rep , and then repeat with the dumbbell in your left hand .
rep : do 10 with each arm .
seat calf raise a. place a step in front of a bench , grab a pair of dumbbell , and sit down .
set the ball of both foot on the step , and hold a dumbbell vertically on each knee .
low both heel as far as you can without touch the floor .
b. push off the ball of your foot and lift your heel as high as you can .
pause and repeat .
rep : 10 to 12 chest - support row a. grab a pair of dumbbell and lie chest down on an adjustable bench set to a low incline .
let the dumbbell hang at arm be length from your shoulder , your palm face each other .
b. without move your torso , pull the weight to your side .
pause , low , and repeat .

cool - down : 5 minute of static stretch , such as hold a hamstring stretch or a calf stretch .
note : adjust the weight and number of repetition to challenge yourself , but maintain good form .
take 1 - 2 minute of rest between set .
drink plenty of water throughout the workout .
eat a healthy diet to support your fitness goal .
this program be design to be challenging , but it be important to listen to your body and rest when you need to .

you be correct that the basic structure of a workout routine can be similar for both novice and expert , with adjustment make for intensity , volume , and complexity of exercise .
however , there be some key difference to consider : novice : focus on form : for beginner , the focus should be on learn the correct form of each exercise to avoid injury and ensure effectiveness .
full - body workout : novice often start with full - body workouts that target all major muscle group in a single session .
this help to build a solid foundation of strength and endurance .
simple exercise : beginner should start with simpler exercise and gradually progress to more complex movement as their strength and skill improve .
rest and recovery : novice may need more rest between workout to allow their body to recover and adapt to the new physical demand .
expert : specific goal : experienced individual often have specific fitness goal , such as increase muscle mass , improve athletic performance , or enhance a particular skill .
their workout routine be tailor to these goal .
split routine : expert often use split routine , where different muscle group be target on different day .
this allow for high volume and intensity per muscle group .
complex movement : experienced individual can safely perform more complex movement that can challenge their body in different way and lead to great gain .
advanced technique : expert can use advanced train technique such as supersets , drop set , and pyramid , which can help to increase intensity and promote muscle growth .
remember , whether you be a novice or an expert , it be important to listen to your body , adjust your workout as need , and consult with a fitness professional to ensure your workout be safe and effective for your fitness level and goal .

then , stand back up .

low your body until your chest nearly touch the floor .
keep your elbow close to your body as you push back up .
lunge ( 1 minute ) : stand tall .
step forward with one foot and low your body until your front knee be at a 90 - degree angle .
push back up and switch leg .
plank ( 1 minute ) : start on your hand and knee .
low your forearm to the floor with elbow position under your shoulder .
hold this position , keep your body in a straight line .
jump jack ( 1 minute ) : stand with your foot together and your hand at your side .
simultaneously raise your arm above your head and jump up just enough to spread your foot wide .
reverse the movement to the start position .
repeat this 5 - exercise circuit twice .
cool - down ( 3 minute ) walk in place for 1 minute to lower your heart rate .
follow with 2 minute of stretch exercise , focus on your major muscle group .
tip make sure to keep your body hydrate .
always maintain proper form to prevent injury .

even a short workout be good than no workout .

resistance band workout : a comprehensive guide resistance band be a versatile and convenient tool for strength training and rehabilitation .
they be lightweight , portable , and come in a variety of resistance level , make them suitable for all fitness level .
what be resistance band ?
resistance band be elastic band use for strength training and physical therapy .
they provide resistance when stretch , allow you to strengthen your muscle without weight .
benefit of resistance band workouts resistance band workouts offer several benefit : versatility : resistance band can be use to perform a wide range of exercise that target different muscle group .
adaptability : they be suitable for all fitness level , as they come in different resistance level .
convenience : resistance band be lightweight and portable , make them ideal for workout at home or on the go .
efficiency : they force you to complete a high - volume workout in a short amount of time .
how to use resistance band when use resistance band , it be important to use proper form and technique to prevent injury and maximize effectiveness .
here be some tip : maintain tension : always keep a slight tension in the band , even in the rest position of an exercise .
control movement : perform each movement in a slow and controlled manner , focus on the muscle you be work .
full range of motion : try to go through a full range of motion during each exercise .
consistent workout : consistency be key .
aim for at least three resistance band workout per week .
sample resistance band workout here be a sample full - body resistance band workout you can try : squat : stand on the band with foot shoulder - width apart , hold handle at shoulder height , and perform squat .
chest press : anchor the band at chest height behind you , hold handle at chest level , and press forward .
row : anchor the band at chest height in front of you , hold handle with arm extend , and pull back .
shoulder press : stand on the band with foot shoulder - width apart , hold handle at shoulder height , and press upward .
bicep curl : stand on the band with foot shoulder - width apart , hold handle with arm extend down , and curl up .
tricep extension : anchor the band at chest height behind you , hold handle with elbows bent at 90 degree , and extend arm .
remember to warm up before start any workout and cool down afterwards .
also , listen to your body and adjust the intensity of the workout to suit your fitness level .
if you be new to work out , you might want to consider get guidance from a fitness professional to ensure you be do the exercise correctly and safely .
resistance band workout be a great way to stay fit and strong , no matter where you be .
so grab your band and get move !

here be some more specific tip and advice for use resistance band : anchor your resistance band securely .
when perform resistance band exercise , it be important to anchor the band securely to a stable object , such as a doorknob , furniture leg , or resistance band anchor .
this will help to ensure that the band do not slip or move during the exercise .
keep the tension on the band .
when perform resistance band exercise , try to keep the tension on the band throughout the entire exercise .
this will help to maximize the muscle activation and benefit of the exercise .
use a variety of resistance band .
resistance band come in a variety of resistance , so it be a good idea to have a set with different resistance .
this will allow you to choose the appropriate resistance band for each exercise and to gradually increase the resistance as you get strong .
use resistance band in combination with other exercise .
resistance band can be use in combination with other exercise , such as weight and bodyweight exercise , to create a more challenging and comprehensive workout .
here be some example of specific resistance band exercise that you can try : squat : wrap a resistance band around your thigh , just above your knee .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and your toe point slightly outward .
squat down until your thigh be parallel to the ground , keep your back straight and your core engage .
drive through your heel to stand back up .
row : wrap a resistance band around a doorknob or other sturdy object .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and your back face the doorknob .
grab the end of the resistance band with each hand and bend over at the waist , keep your back straight .
row the resistance band up to your chest , keep your elbow close to your side .
slowly low the resistance band back to the start position .
overhead press : wrap a resistance band behind your back , with each hand hold an end of the band .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and your knee slightly bend .
press the resistance band overhead , keep your elbow straight .
slowly low the resistance band back to the start position .
lunge : wrap a resistance band around your ankle .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and step forward with one leg , bend both knee until your front thigh be parallel to the ground .
keep your back straight and your core engage .
drive through your front heel to stand back up .
repeat with the other leg .
bicep curl : wrap a resistance band around a sturdy object .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and grab an end of the resistance band with each hand .
curl the resistance band up to your shoulder , keep your elbow close to your side .
slowly low the resistance band back to the start position .
tricep extension : wrap a resistance band behind your head , with each hand hold an end of the band .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and extend your arm overhead , keep your elbow slightly bend .
extend your arm behind your head , straighten your elbow .
slowly return to the start position .
these be just a few example of resistance band exercise .
there be many other exercise that you can perform use resistance band .
you can find more resistance band exercise online and in fitness book and magazine .
resistance band be a great way to get a full - body workout at home or on the go .
they be also a great option for people of all fitness level .
by follow the tip and advice above , you can safely and effectively use resistance band to achieve your fitness goal .
here be some more specific resistance band exercise that you can try : chest resistance band bench press : wrap a resistance band around your back , with each hand hold an end of the band .
lie on your back on a bench or the floor , with your foot flat on the ground and your knee bent .
press the resistance band up to your chest , keep your elbow close to your side .
slowly low the resistance band back to the start position .
resistance band fly : wrap a resistance band around your back , with each hand hold an end of the band .
lie on your back on a bench or the floor , with your foot flat on the ground and your knee bent .
spread your arm out to the side , keep your elbow slightly bend .
slowly low your arm back to the start position .
back resistance band pull - ups : wrap a resistance band over a pull - up bar or other sturdy object .
grab an end of the resistance band with each hand and hang from the pull - up bar , with your arm fully extend .
pull yourself up to the bar , keep your elbow close to your side .
slowly low yourself back to the start position .
resistance band seat cable row : wrap a resistance band around a sturdy object , such as a doorknob or furniture leg .
sit on the floor with your leg extend in front of you and grab an end of the resistance band with each hand .
bend forward at the waist , keep your back straight .
row the resistance band up to your chest , keep your elbow close to your side .
slowly low the resistance band back to the start position .
shoulder resistance band lateral raise : wrap a resistance band around your foot .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and grab an end of the resistance band with each hand .
raise your arm out to the side , keep your elbow slightly bend .
slowly low your arm back to the start position .
resistance band front raise : wrap a resistance band around your foot .
stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and grab an end of the resistance band with each hand .
raise your arm in front of you , keep your elbow slightly bend .
slowly low your arm back to the start position .
leg resistance band hip thrust : wrap a resistance band around your hip , just above your knee .
lie on your back on the floor with your foot flat on the ground and your knee bent .
thrust your hip up off the floor until your body form a straight line from your shoulder to your knee .
slowly low yourself back to the start position .
resistance band hamstring curl : wrap a resistance band around your ankle .
lie on your back on the floor with your foot flat on the ground and your knee bent .
curl your heel up towards your glute , keep your knee bent .
slowly low your heel back to the start position .
these be just a few more example of resistance band exercise .
there be many other exercise that you can perform use resistance band .
you can find more resistance band exercise online and in fitness book and magazine .
benefit versatility : bodyweight workout can be do anywhere , anytime , without any equipment .
this make them a great option for people who travel frequently or who do not have access to a gym .
efficiency : bodyweight workout be very efficient , mean that you can get a great workout in a short amount of time .
this be because bodyweight workout typically involve compound exercise that work multiple muscle group at the same time .
functional fitness : bodyweight workout can help to improve your functional fitness , which be the ability to perform everyday task with ease .
this be because bodyweight workout often mimic everyday movement , such as squatting , lunging , and push .
injury prevention : bodyweight workout can help to prevent injury by strengthen your muscle and joint .
this be because bodyweight workout typically focus on core strength , balance , and stability .
advice start slowly : if you be new to bodyweight workout , start slowly and gradually increase the intensity and duration of your workout over time .
this will help to prevent injury .
focus on form : it be important to focus on proper form when perform bodyweight exercise .
this will help you to get the most out of the exercise and prevent injury .
use progression and regression : if you find an exercise too difficult , there be often regression that you can do .
for example , if you ca not do a full push - up , you can do a knee push - up .
conversely , if you find an exercise too easy , there be often progression that you can do .
for example , if you can do regular push - ups , you can try do incline push - ups or decline push - ups .
make it challenge : to get the most out of your bodyweight workout , make sure to challenge yourself .
you can do this by increase the intensity and duration of your workout , or by add weight or resistance .
here be some additional tip for get the most out of your bodyweight workout : warm up before each workout .
a good warm - up will help to prepare your body for exercise and reduce your risk of injury .
some example of warm - up exercise include light cardio , dynamic stretch , and joint rotation .
cool down after each workout .
a cool - down will help your body to recover from exercise and prevent soreness .
some example of cool - down exercise include static stretch and light cardio .

here be some specific bodyweight exercise that you can try : squat : squat work your quadriceps , hamstring , glute , and core .
to perform a squat , stand with your foot shoulder - width apart and low your body down until your thigh be parallel to the ground .
keep your back straight and your core engage .
drive through your heel to stand back up .
lunge : lunge work your quadriceps , hamstring , glute , and core .
to perform a lunge , step forward with one leg and low your body down until both knee be bent at a 90 - degree angle .
keep your back straight and your core engage .
drive through your front heel to stand back up .
repeat with the other leg .
push - ups : push - ups work your chest , triceps , shoulder , and core .
to perform a push - up , start in a plank position with your hand shoulder - width apart and your body in a straight line from your head to your heel .
low your body down until your chest touch the ground .
keep your back straight and your core engage .
push back up to the start position .
pull - ups : pull - ups work your back , biceps , and forearm .
to perform a pull - up , grab a pull - up bar with an overhand grip , shoulder - width apart .
hang from the bar with your arm fully extend .
pull yourself up to the bar until your chin be over the bar .
slowly low yourself back to the start position .

you can find more bodyweight exercise online and in fitness book and magazine .

weight loss workout vs. form of exercise : a contrast exercise be a key component of any fitness regimen , but not all workout be create equal .
different form of exercise serve different purpose , and understand these difference can help you tailor your workout routine to your specific goal .
in this essay , we will contrast weight loss workout with other form of exercise , focus on the execution of each movement , include speed , tempo , rest , and rep count .
weight loss workout weight loss workout be typically characterize by high - intensity , fast - paced exercise that aim to burn calorie and fat .
the goal be to elevate the heart rate and keep it elevate for extend period , which increase the body be metabolic rate and lead to great calorie burn .
speed : weight loss workout often involve quick , explosive movement .
the faster you move , the more calorie you burn .
tempo : the tempo of weight loss workout be typically fast .
this help to keep the heart rate elevate and maintain a high level of intensity .
rest : rest period in weight loss workout be usually short , often range from 30 second to a minute .
the goal be to keep the heart rate elevate and maintain the intensity of the workout .
rep count : weight loss workout often involve high rep count .
the idea be to perform as many rep as possible within a give time frame to maximize calorie burn .
form of exercise form of exercise , such as strength training or flexibility exercise , have different goal and therefore different execution parameter .
speed : in contrast to weight loss workout , other form of exercise often involve slow , more controlled movement .
this allow for great focus on form and muscle engagement .
tempo : the tempo of these workout be typically slow , allow for a great focus on muscle contraction and relaxation .
rest : rest period in these workout be often longer , range from one to three minute .
this allow the muscle to recover and prepare for the next set .
rep count : these workout often involve low rep count , typically range from 5 to 15 rep per set .
the focus be on quality of movement rather than quantity .
in conclusion , while all form of exercise can contribute to overall fitness , the specific goal of a workout will dictate its execution .
weight loss workout be characterize by high intensity , fast tempo , short rest period , and high rep count , design to maximize calorie burn and promote weight loss .
form of exercise , on the other hand , may prioritize muscle strength , endurance , or flexibility , and therefore involve slow , more controlled movement , long rest period , and low rep count .
understand these difference can help you tailor your workout routine to your specific fitness goal .

these exercise may not improve your endurance or strength , but be flexible give you more freedom of movement for other exercise as well as for your everyday activity .

for example , if you have a knee injury , you can modify squat by do them against a wall or with a chair .

this can reduce the stress on your joint and muscle .
